* The identity of [Cleo](/wiki/Cleo_%28mathematician%29 "Cleo (mathematician)") is revealed to be Vladimir Reshetnikov, an [Uzbek](/wiki/Uzbeks "Uzbeks") software developer, after a decade of mystery. [(Meduza)](https://leudqmqvebuspimd.1tw.live/feature/2025/02/20/polzovateli-bolshe-desyati-let-vyyasnyali-lichnost-genialnoy-zhenschiny-matematika-kleo)

**Sports**

* [2025 4 Nations Face-Off](/wiki/2025_4_Nations_Face-Off "2025 4 Nations Face-Off")
  + Amidst [heightened tensions](/wiki/Canada%E2%80%93United_States_relations "Canada–United States relations") between the two nations, the [Canadian](/wiki/Canada "Canada") [men's ice hockey team](/wiki/Canada_men%27s_national_ice_hockey_team "Canada men's national ice hockey team") defeats the [United States team](/wiki/United_States_men%27s_national_ice_hockey_team "United States men's national ice hockey team") 3–2 in [overtime](/wiki/Overtime_%28sports%29 "Overtime (sports)") in the final of the [4 Nations Face-Off](/wiki/2025_4_Nations_Face-Off "2025 4 Nations Face-Off"), with [Connor McDavid](/wiki/Connor_McDavid "Connor McDavid") scoring the winning goal. [(BBC)](https://www.bbc.com/news/articles/ce8ydg04xezo) [(NPR)](https://www.npr.org/2025/02/21/g-s1-50085/canada-united-states-hockey-four-nations-face-off-connor-mcdavid-51st-state)

February 21, 2025 (2025-02-21) (Friday)

* [edit](https://en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Portal:Current_events/2025_February_21&action=edit&editintro=Portal:Current_events/Edit_instructions)
* [history](https://en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Portal:Current_events/2025_February_21&action=history)
* [watch](https://en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Portal:Current_events/2025_February_21&action=watch)

**Armed conflicts and attacks**

* [Gaza war](/wiki/Gaza_war "Gaza war")
  + [2025 Gaza war ceasefire](/wiki/2025_Gaza_war_ceasefire "2025 Gaza war ceasefire"), [Gaza war hostage crisis](/wiki/Gaza_war_hostage_crisis "Gaza war hostage crisis")
    - [Israel](/wiki/Israel "Israel") says that forensic testing revealed one of the bodies returned by [Hamas](/wiki/Hamas "Hamas") yesterday does not match with [Shiri Bibas](/wiki/Kidnapping_of_the_Bibas_family "Kidnapping of the Bibas family") nor with any other hostages. Her sons Ariel and Kfir, as well as [Oded Lifshitz](/wiki/Oded_Lifshitz "Oded Lifshitz"), were all positively identified. Israel accuses Hamas of violating the ceasefire and demands the return of her body along with the other remaining hostages. [(BBC News)](https://www.bbc.com/news/articles/cjry3jzedl1o)
    - Hamas claims that Shiri's body was "mistakenly mixed" with others who were killed and buried under the rubble in [Gaza](/wiki/Gaza_Strip "Gaza Strip"), and returns an additional body the group says is hers. The identity is soon afterwards positively confirmed by Israel. [(Al Arabiya)](https://english.alarabiya.net/News/middle-east/2025/02/21/hamas-says-shiri-bibas-remains-mixed-with-other-human-remains-after-israeli-airstrike) [(BBC News)](https://www.bbc.com/news/articles/cjw20d3l4jpo)

**Business and economy**

* [2025 United States federal mass layoffs](/wiki/2025_United_States_federal_mass_layoffs "2025 United States federal mass layoffs")
  + The [United States](/wiki/United_States "United States") [Department of Defense](/wiki/Department_of_Defense_%28United_States%29 "Department of Defense (United States)") announces it will jointly [lay off](/wiki/Layoff "Layoff") 4,500 [probationary workers](/wiki/Probation_%28workplace%29 "Probation (workplace)"), cutting 5-8% of the [civilian workforce](/wiki/United_States_federal_civil_service "United States federal civil service"). The [United States Forest Service](/wiki/United_States_Forest_Service "United States Forest Service") also announces it will lay off 2,000 employees. [(AP)](https://apnews.com/article/pentagon-job-cuts-trump-doge-31e3ed62f5f35a5e5a4a07fd8708232f)
* The [Financial Action Task Force](/wiki/Financial_Action_Task_Force "Financial Action Task Force") removes the [Philippines](/wiki/Philippines "Philippines") from its [grey list](/wiki/FATF_grey_list "FATF grey list") and adds [Laos](/wiki/Laos "Laos") and [Nepal](/wiki/Nepal "Nepal") to the list. [(Reuters)](https://www.reuters.com/world/fatf-global-financial-crime-watchdog-removes-philippines-grey-list-2025-02-21/)

**Disasters and accidents**

* [Real Plaza Trujillo collapse](/wiki/Real_Plaza_Trujillo_collapse "Real Plaza Trujillo collapse")
  + At least 6 people are killed and 79 others are injured after a roof collapses at the [Real Plaza Trujillo](/wiki/Real_Plaza_Trujillo "Real Plaza Trujillo") [shopping mall](/wiki/Shopping_mall "Shopping mall") in [Trujillo](/wiki/Trujillo%2C_Peru "Trujillo, Peru"), [Peru](/wiki/Peru "Peru"). [(*Metro*)](https://metro.co.uk/2025/02/22/shopping-centre-roof-collapses-killing-least-3-including-child-injuring-79-22606215/)

* Twelve people are killed and twenty-one others were injured in a bus crash in [São Paulo](/wiki/S%C3%A3o_Paulo_%28state%29 "São Paulo (state)"), [Brazil](/wiki/Brazil "Brazil"). [(TRT World)](https://www.trtworld.com/latin-america/twelve-university-students-killed-in-brazil-bus-crash-officials-18267535/)

**Health and environment**

* [South Sudan](/wiki/South_Sudan "South Sudan") orders the closure of all schools in the country for two weeks due to a [heat wave](/wiki/Heat_wave "Heat wave"), with temperatures expected to reach 42 °C (108 °F). [(DW)](https://www.dw.com/en/heat-wave-forces-south-sudan-to-close-schools-for-two-weeks/a-71698826)
* A [norovirus](/wiki/Norovirus "Norovirus") outbreak with a large number of ill passengers is reported on the [MS Iona](/wiki/MS_Iona "MS Iona") cruise ship in [Belgium](/wiki/Belgium "Belgium"). [(*Metro*)](https://metro.co.uk/2025/02/21/cruise-passengers-dropping-like-flies-norovirus-outbreak-22605507/)

**International relations**

* [2025 Gaza war ceasefire](/wiki/2025_Gaza_war_ceasefire "2025 Gaza war ceasefire")
  + [Egypt](/wiki/Egypt "Egypt"), [Jordan](/wiki/Jordan "Jordan"), and the countries of the [Gulf Cooperation Council](/wiki/Gulf_Cooperation_Council "Gulf Cooperation Council") meet in [Riyadh](/wiki/Riyadh "Riyadh"), [Saudi Arabia](/wiki/Saudi_Arabia "Saudi Arabia"), to address possible future developments in the [Gaza Strip](/wiki/Gaza_Strip "Gaza Strip"). [(*The Times of Israel*)](https://www.timesofisrael.com/arab-leaders-gather-in-saudi-arabia-to-hash-out-alternative-to-trumps-plan-for-gaza/)
* [Kyrgyzstan–Tajikistan relations](/wiki/Kyrgyzstan%E2%80%93Tajikistan_relations "Kyrgyzstan–Tajikistan relations")
  + [Kyrgyzstan](/wiki/Kyrgyzstan "Kyrgyzstan") and [Tajikistan](/wiki/Tajikistan "Tajikistan") sign an agreement to [delimitate](/wiki/National_boundary_delimitation "National boundary delimitation") [their border](/wiki/Kyrgyzstan%E2%80%93Tajikistan_border "Kyrgyzstan–Tajikistan border"), solving a decades-old [border dispute](/wiki/Territorial_disputes "Territorial disputes") that had sparked clashes between different ethnic groups that had killed over a hundred people. [(Trend News Agency)](https://en.trend.az/casia/kyrgyzstan/4008880.html) [(Reuters)](https://www.reuters.com/world/asia-pacific/kyrgyzstan-tajikistan-settle-border-dispute-that-sparked-deadly-clashes-2025-02-21/)

**Law and crime**

* [2024 South Korean martial law crisis](/wiki/2024_South_Korean_martial_law_crisis "2024 South Korean martial law crisis")
  + [Arrest of Yoon Suk Yeol](/wiki/Arrest_of_Yoon_Suk_Yeol "Arrest of Yoon Suk Yeol")
    - [South Korean police](/wiki/Police_of_South_Korea "Police of South Korea") file a case against [impeached](/wiki/Impeachment_of_Yoon_Suk_Yeol "Impeachment of Yoon Suk Yeol") [president](/wiki/President_of_South_Korea "President of South Korea") [Yoon Suk Yeol](/wiki/Yoon_Suk_Yeol "Yoon Suk Yeol") for obstructing [his arrest warrant](/wiki/Arrest_of_Yoon_Suk_Yeol "Arrest of Yoon Suk Yeol"). [(Reuters)](https://www.reuters.com/world/asia-pacific/south-korea-police-say-building-case-against-yoon-obstructing-arrest-2025-02-21/)
* [Berlin Holocaust memorial stabbing](/wiki/Berlin_Holocaust_memorial_stabbing "Berlin Holocaust memorial stabbing")
  + A 30-year-old [Spanish](/wiki/Spain "Spain") tourist is seriously injured in a [stabbing attack](/wiki/Berlin_Holocaust_memorial_stabbing "Berlin Holocaust memorial stabbing") at the [Memorial to the Murdered Jews of Europe](/wiki/Memorial_to_the_Murdered_Jews_of_Europe "Memorial to the Murdered Jews of Europe") in [Berlin](/wiki/Berlin "Berlin"), [Germany](/wiki/Germany "Germany"). A 19-year-old Syrian man is arrested. [(AP)](https://apnews.com/article/germany-berlin-stabbing-holocaust-memorial-1710be90a0e733d016e32db4d8353e1c) [(DW)](https://www.dw.com/en/suspect-in-berlin-stabbing-wanted-to-kill-jews-police/a-71712971)
* [Flint water crisis](/wiki/Flint_water_crisis "Flint water crisis")
  + [Veolia Water](/wiki/Veolia_Water "Veolia Water") agrees to pay $53 million in [settlement](/wiki/Settlement_%28litigation%29 "Settlement (litigation)") for all remaining active [class action](/wiki/Class_action "Class action") [lawsuits](/wiki/Lawsuit "Lawsuit") for the [contamination](/wiki/Water_pollution "Water pollution") of [drinking water](/wiki/Drinking_water "Drinking water") in [Flint](/wiki/Flint%2C_Michigan "Flint, Michigan"), [Michigan](/wiki/Michigan "Michigan"), United States, but refuses to acknowledge any fault in the crisis. [(AP)](https://apnews.com/article/flint-water-settlement-lead-3cadd9eb6ffbd699159c992de9cdbc27) [(WNEM)](https://www.wnem.com/2025/02/21/53m-civil-settlement-reached-flint-water-crisis-lawsuit/)
* [Stabbing of Salman Rushdie](/wiki/Stabbing_of_Salman_Rushdie#Criminal_investigation_and_prosecution "Stabbing of Salman Rushdie")
  + Hadi Matar is found guilty by a [U.S. jury](/wiki/Juries_in_the_United_States "Juries in the United States") of [attempted murder](/wiki/Attempted_murder "Attempted murder") and [assault](/wiki/Assault "Assault") for his [stabbing attack](/wiki/Stabbing_attack "Stabbing attack") on author [Salman Rushdie](/wiki/Salman_Rushdie "Salman Rushdie") in 2022. [(ABC News)](https://abcnews.go.com/US/salman-rushdie-stabbing-suspect-found-guilty-attempted-murder/story?id=118903519)
* Three people are killed in a shooting outside of a [motor vehicle office](/wiki/Department_of_motor_vehicles "Department of motor vehicles") in [Louisville, Kentucky](/wiki/Louisville%2C_Kentucky "Louisville, Kentucky"), United States. [(*The Independent*)](https://www.independent.co.uk/news/world/americas/crime/louisville-shooting-three-dead-willismore-b2702549.html)
* Three people, including two [police officers](/wiki/Virginia_Beach_Police_Department "Virginia Beach Police Department"), are killed during a traffic stop in [Virginia Beach](/wiki/Virginia_Beach%2C_Virginia "Virginia Beach, Virginia"), [Virginia](/wiki/Virginia "Virginia"), United States. [(*The New York Times*)](https://www.nytimes.com/2025/02/22/us/virginia-beach-police-shooting.html?searchResultPosition=1)
* The [Supreme Federal Court](/wiki/Supreme_Federal_Court "Supreme Federal Court") of [Brazil](/wiki/Brazil "Brazil") orders the suspension of [online video platform](/wiki/Online_video_platform "Online video platform") [Rumble](/wiki/Rumble_%28company%29 "Rumble (company)") for [refusing to comply](/wiki/Contempt_of_court "Contempt of court") to court orders and for refusing to remove the account of Brazilian [fugitive](/wiki/Fugitive "Fugitive") [Allan dos Santos](/wiki/Allan_dos_Santos "Allan dos Santos"). [(AP)](https://apnews.com/article/brazil-supreme-court-rumble-blocked-c45ab801d5bb23e6d9b2271bdcf7426e)

**Politics and elections**

* [Second presidency of Donald Trump](/wiki/Second_presidency_of_Donald_Trump "Second presidency of Donald Trump")
  + [U.S. President](/wiki/U.S._President "U.S. President") [Donald Trump](/wiki/Donald_Trump "Donald Trump") and [Secretary of Defense](/wiki/United_States_Secretary_of_Defense "United States Secretary of Defense") [Pete Hegseth](/wiki/Pete_Hegseth "Pete Hegseth") announces the removal of multiple senior U.S. officers from their current roles, including the [Chairman of the Joint Chiefs of Staff](/wiki/Chairman_of_the_Joint_Chiefs_of_Staff "Chairman of the Joint Chiefs of Staff") [Charles Q. Brown Jr.](/wiki/Charles_Q._Brown_Jr. "Charles Q. Brown Jr.") and the [Chief of Naval Operations](/wiki/Chief_of_Naval_Operations "Chief of Naval Operations") [Lisa Franchetti](/wiki/Lisa_Franchetti "Lisa Franchetti"). [(CNN)](https://www.cnn.com/2025/02/21/politics/trump-fires-top-us-general-cq-brown/index.html)
  + American [news agency](/wiki/News_agency "News agency") [The Associated Press](/wiki/The_Associated_Press "The Associated Press") files a lawsuit for [freedom of speech](/wiki/Freedom_of_speech_in_the_United_States "Freedom of speech in the United States") against three [Trump administration](/wiki/Second_presidency_of_Donald_Trump "Second presidency of Donald Trump") officials after they banned the news agency from attending [presidential press events](/wiki/White_House_press_corps "White House press corps") after the agency refused to refer to the [Gulf of Mexico](/wiki/Gulf_of_Mexico "Gulf of Mexico") as the "Gulf of America". [(AP)](https://apnews.com/article/ap-lawsuit-trump-administration-officials-0352075501b779b8b187667f3427e0e8) [(NPR)](https://www.npr.org/2025/02/21/nx-s1-5305226/ap-sues-white-house-gulf-of-america-mexico-trump)
* [Indonesia Gelap](/wiki/Indonesia_Gelap "Indonesia Gelap")
  + Demonstrations continue against [the government](/wiki/Government_of_Indonesia "Government of Indonesia") in several cities in [Indonesia](/wiki/Indonesia "Indonesia"). Nine students have been arrested and two are injured, along with four injured [policemen](/wiki/Indonesian_National_Police "Indonesian National Police") and two [parliament members](/wiki/House_of_Representatives_%28Indonesia%29 "House of Representatives (Indonesia)"). [(*Tempo*)](https://en.tempo.co/read/1978141/police-deploy-2460-joint-personnel-for-indonesia-gelap-protest-in-jakarta-today) [(*Barron's*)](https://www.barrons.com/news/thousands-protest-against-budget-cuts-in-indonesia-5ac272a2)

**Science and technology**

* The [European Space Agency](/wiki/European_Space_Agency "European Space Agency") announces that the chances of [asteroid](/wiki/Asteroid "Asteroid") [2024 YR4](/wiki/2024_YR4 "2024 YR4") impacting [Earth](/wiki/Earth "Earth") in 2032 has decreased to 1.5% (1-in-67), and is likely to decrease further to less than 1%. [(*Nature*)](https://www.nature.com/articles/d41586-025-00552-y)

February 22, 2025 (2025-02-22) (Saturday)

* [edit](https://en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Portal:Current_events/2025_February_22&action=edit&editintro=Portal:Current_events/Edit_instructions)
* [history](https://en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Portal:Current_events/2025_February_22&action=history)

**Armed conflicts and attacks**

* [Gaza war](/wiki/Gaza_war "Gaza war")
  + [2025 Gaza war ceasefire](/wiki/2025_Gaza_war_ceasefire "2025 Gaza war ceasefire"), [Gaza war hostage crisis](/wiki/Gaza_war_hostage_crisis "Gaza war hostage crisis")
    - [Hamas](/wiki/Hamas "Hamas") releases six living hostages, including pre-war hostages [Avera Mengistu](/wiki/Avera_Mengistu "Avera Mengistu") and [Hisham al-Sayed](/wiki/Hisham_al-Sayed "Hisham al-Sayed"), both captive for more than nine years. [(*Times of Israel*)](https://www.timesofisrael.com/these-are-the-six-living-hostages-set-to-be-released-saturday/)
    - [Israeli](/wiki/Israel "Israel") [Prime Minister](/wiki/Prime_Minister_of_Israel "Prime Minister of Israel") [Benjamin Netanyahu](/wiki/Benjamin_Netanyahu "Benjamin Netanyahu") orders the delay of the release of 620 [Palestinian](/wiki/Palestinians "Palestinians") [prisoners](/wiki/Palestinian_prisoners_in_Israel "Palestinian prisoners in Israel") indefinitely, citing the "humiliating" procedure of the hostages' release. [(AP)](https://apnews.com/article/israel-palestinians-hamas-war-ceasefire-hostages-02-22-2025-364c7abeb679e910cb5acba234469574) [(NBC News)](https://www.nbcnews.com/news/world/live-blog/israel-hamas-ceasefire-live-updates-rcna193120)
* [Islamic terrorism in Europe](/wiki/Islamic_terrorism_in_Europe "Islamic terrorism in Europe")
  + [2025 Mulhouse stabbing attack](/wiki/2025_Mulhouse_stabbing_attack "2025 Mulhouse stabbing attack")
    - A 69-year-old [Portuguese](/wiki/Portugal "Portugal") [Lino Sousa Loureiro](/wiki/Lino_Sousa_Loureiro "Lino Sousa Loureiro") is killed and seven other people are injured in a [mass stabbing](/wiki/Mass_stabbing "Mass stabbing") attack by a 37-year-old Algerian man at a market in [Mulhouse](/wiki/Mulhouse "Mulhouse"), [France](/wiki/France "France"). The stabbing is being treated as a suspected [Islamic terrorist](/wiki/Islamic_terrorism "Islamic terrorism") attack. [(AP)](https://apnews.com/article/france-stabbing-islamic-extremism-mulhouse-f360a94b520b199cdd7f389e6ff5e01c) [(CNN)](https://edition.cnn.com/2025/02/22/europe/mulhouse-attack-intl-latam/index.html)
* [Kivu conflict](/wiki/Kivu_conflict "Kivu conflict")
  + [2025 Bukavu offensive](/wiki/2025_Bukavu_offensive "2025 Bukavu offensive")
    - Hundreds of [Congolese police officers](/wiki/Congolese_National_Police "Congolese National Police") join the [M23 movement](/wiki/March_23_Movement "March 23 Movement") in [Bukavu](/wiki/Bukavu "Bukavu"), [Democratic Republic of the Congo](/wiki/Democratic_Republic_of_the_Congo "Democratic Republic of the Congo"), as the rebel group consolidates its control of the city. Around 1,800 police officers have surrendered their weapons to the new authorities, according to the [Congo River Alliance](/wiki/Congo_River_Alliance "Congo River Alliance"). [(Reuters)](https://www.reuters.com/world/africa/hundreds-congolese-police-join-rebels-occupied-city-2025-02-22/)
* [Yemeni civil war](/wiki/Yemeni_civil_war_%282014%E2%80%93present%29 "Yemeni civil war (2014–present)")
  + [Operation Prosperity Guardian](/wiki/Operation_Prosperity_Guardian "Operation Prosperity Guardian")
    - [Houthi forces](/wiki/Houthis "Houthis") launch [surface-to-air missiles](/wiki/Surface-to-air_missile "Surface-to-air missile") at a [U.S.](/wiki/United_States_Air_Force "United States Air Force") fighter jet and [MQ-9 Reaper](/wiki/General_Atomics_MQ-9_Reaper "General Atomics MQ-9 Reaper") drone over the [Red Sea](/wiki/Red_Sea "Red Sea") for the first time with both missiles missing their target. [(Reuters)](https://www.reuters.com/world/middle-east/yemens-houthis-launched-missile-us-fighter-jet-missed-2025-02-22/)
* [Mali War](/wiki/Mali_War "Mali War")
  + The [Tuareg](/wiki/Tuareg_people "Tuareg people") [independence movement](/wiki/National_Movement_for_the_Liberation_of_Azawad "National Movement for the Liberation of Azawad") accuses [Malian soldiers](/wiki/Malian_Armed_Forces "Malian Armed Forces") and [Wagner Group](/wiki/Wagner_Group "Wagner Group") mercenaries of killing 24 civilians, which constitutes a [war crime](/wiki/War_crime "War crime"). [(Al Jazeera)](https://www.aljazeera.com/news/2025/2/22/malis-army-says-investigating-soldiers-accused-of-killing-24-civilians)

**Arts and culture**

* [75th Berlin International Film Festival](/wiki/75th_Berlin_International_Film_Festival "75th Berlin International Film Festival")
  + [Norwegian](/wiki/Cinema_of_Norway "Cinema of Norway") [drama film](/wiki/Drama_%28film_and_television%29 "Drama (film and television)") *[Dreams (Sex Love)](/wiki/Dreams_%28Sex_Love%29 "Dreams (Sex Love)")* wins the [Golden Bear](/wiki/Golden_Bear "Golden Bear") award at the 2025 [Berlin International Film Festival](/wiki/Berlin_International_Film_Festival "Berlin International Film Festival"), while [Tilda Swinton](/wiki/Tilda_Swinton "Tilda Swinton") is awarded the [Honorary Golden Bear](/wiki/Honorary_Golden_Bear "Honorary Golden Bear") for her range and [legacy](/wiki/Tilda_Swinton_filmography "Tilda Swinton filmography"). [(DW)](https://www.dw.com/en/coming-of-age-film-from-norway-wins-berlinales-golden-bear/a-71716079) [(Berlinale)](https://www.berlinale.de/en/festival/awards-and-juries/honorary-golden-bear.html)

**Disasters and accidents**

* [Real Plaza Trujillo roof collapse](/wiki/Real_Plaza_Trujillo_roof_collapse "Real Plaza Trujillo roof collapse")
  + The death toll following the [structural collapse](/wiki/Structural_integrity_and_failure "Structural integrity and failure") of a metal roof of the [Real Plaza Trujillo](/wiki/Real_Plaza_Trujillo "Real Plaza Trujillo") in [Trujillo](/wiki/Trujillo%2C_Peru "Trujillo, Peru"), [Peru](/wiki/Peru "Peru"), rises to eight. The [La Libertad](/wiki/Department_of_La_Libertad "Department of La Libertad") government announces a period of mourning from February 22–23. [(*La Republica*)](https://larepublica.pe/sociedad/2025/02/21/colapsa-techo-de-real-plaza-en-trujillo-en-vivo-reporte-de-heridos-y-ultimas-noticias-segun-coer-1782711)
* A bus carrying passengers to a wedding ceremony overturns in Ranhghati, [Rajasthan](/wiki/Rajasthan "Rajasthan"), [India](/wiki/India "India"), killing two people and injuring 30 others. [(*The Times of India*)](https://timesofindia.indiatimes.com/city/jaipur/two-dead-30-injured-as-bus-overturns/articleshow/118487309.cms)
* A bus crashed into a petrol tanker in [Niger State](/wiki/Niger_State "Niger State"), killing 14 and injuring six. [(ARAB NEWS)](https://www.arabnews.com/node/2591303/world)

**International relations**

* [China–Cook Islands relations](/wiki/China%E2%80%93Cook_Islands_relations "China–Cook Islands relations")
  + The [Cook Islands](/wiki/Cook_Islands "Cook Islands") signs a five-year [memorandum of understanding](/wiki/Memorandum_of_understanding "Memorandum of understanding") to collaborate with [China](/wiki/China "China") in [seabed mining](/wiki/Seabed_mining "Seabed mining"), which includes [technology transfer](/wiki/Technology_transfer "Technology transfer"), [logistics](/wiki/Logistics "Logistics") support, and [deep-sea](/wiki/Deep-sea_community "Deep-sea community") [ecosystem](/wiki/Marine_ecosystem "Marine ecosystem") research. [(DW)](https://www.dw.com/en/cook-islands-announces-deep-sea-minerals-deal-with-china/a-71711275) [(*The Guardian*)](https://www.theguardian.com/world/2025/feb/22/cook-islands-china-partnership-response)

**Law and crime**

* [UPMC Memorial Hospital shooting](/wiki/UPMC_Memorial_Hospital_shooting "UPMC Memorial Hospital shooting")
  + Two people, including a police officer, are killed and seven other people are injured in a [mass shooting](/wiki/Mass_shooting "Mass shooting") at the UPMC Memorial Hospital in [West Manchester Township](/wiki/West_Manchester_Township%2C_Pennsylvania "West Manchester Township, Pennsylvania"), [York County](/wiki/York_County%2C_Pennsylvania "York County, Pennsylvania"), [Pennsylvania](/wiki/Pennsylvania "Pennsylvania"), United States. [(*York Daily Record*)](https://www.ydr.com/story/news/crime/2025/02/22/shooter-targeted-the-icu-at-upmc-memorial-killing-a-police-officer/79682914007/) [(Fox News)](https://www.fox43.com/article/news/local/york-county/police-incident-upmc-york-public-to-avoid-the-area/521-0c7355f3-6262-4ef5-8b76-9353775cabf9)
* One person is killed and another is injured in a shooting at the [Kirtland Air Force Base](/wiki/Kirtland_Air_Force_Base "Kirtland Air Force Base") in [Albuquerque](/wiki/Albuquerque "Albuquerque"), [New Mexico](/wiki/New_Mexico "New Mexico"), United States. The [FBI](/wiki/Federal_Bureau_of_Investigation "Federal Bureau of Investigation") is investigating the shooting but it is believed the incident was not an act of [terrorism](/wiki/Terrorism "Terrorism"). [(ABC News)](https://abcnews.go.com/US/wireStory/shooting-air-force-base-new-mexico-kills-airman-119079724)
* [Mohamed Amra](/wiki/Mohamed_Amra "Mohamed Amra"), a [French](/wiki/France "France") criminal and suspected [drug lord](/wiki/Drug_lord "Drug lord") known as "The Fly", is recaptured in [Romania](/wiki/Romania "Romania"), nine months after escaping during an ambush that killed two French prison officers. [(Sky News)](https://news.sky.com/story/mohamed-amra-the-fly-recaptured-in-romania-nine-months-after-escape-that-killed-two-french-prison-officers-13314864)

**Politics and elections**

* The [Vatican City](/wiki/Vatican_City "Vatican City") issues a statement informing of the worsening health of [Pope Francis](/wiki/Pope_Francis "Pope Francis") after more than a week in hospital due to [respiratory problems](/wiki/Respiratory_disease "Respiratory disease"). Vatican officials say Pope Francis is now in [critical condition](/wiki/Critical_condition "Critical condition") and that the prognosis "remains guarded". [(Reuters)](https://www.reuters.com/world/europe/pope-francis-will-not-lead-sunday-prayers-second-week-running-vatican-says-2025-02-22/)

February 23, 2025 (2025-02-23) (Sunday)

* [edit](https://en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Portal:Current_events/2025_February_23&action=edit&editintro=Portal:Current_events/Edit_instructions)
* [history](https://en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Portal:Current_events/2025_February_23&action=history)
* [watch](https://en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Portal:Current_events/2025_February_23&action=watch)

**Armed conflicts and attacks**

* [Israeli–Palestinian conflict](/wiki/Israeli%E2%80%93Palestinian_conflict "Israeli–Palestinian conflict")
  + [Israeli occupation of the West Bank](/wiki/Israeli_occupation_of_the_West_Bank "Israeli occupation of the West Bank")
    - [2025 Israeli operation in the West Bank](/wiki/2025_Israeli_operation_in_the_West_Bank "2025 Israeli operation in the West Bank")
      * The [Israel Defense Forces](/wiki/Israel_Defense_Forces "Israel Defense Forces") deploy [tanks](/wiki/Armored_Corps_%28Israel%29 "Armored Corps (Israel)") into the [West Bank](/wiki/West_Bank "West Bank") for the first time since [2002](/wiki/Second_Intifada "Second Intifada"), declaring that the 40,000 [Palestinians](/wiki/Palestinians "Palestinians") who fled [refugee camps](/wiki/Palestinian_refugee_camps "Palestinian refugee camps") in the region cannot [return](/wiki/Palestinian_right_of_return "Palestinian right of return"). [(AP)](https://apnews.com/article/israel-palestinians-hamas-war-ceasefire-hostages-02-23-2025-1c2dc86afd2e05888d5d588f462e898b) [(PBS)](https://www.pbs.org/newshour/world/amid-growing-crackdown-israeli-tanks-enter-occupied-west-bank-for-the-first-time-since-2002)
* [War against the Islamic State](/wiki/War_against_the_Islamic_State "War against the Islamic State")
  + [Islamic State insurgency in Puntland](/wiki/Islamic_State_insurgency_in_Puntland "Islamic State insurgency in Puntland")
    - [Puntland counter-terrorism operations](/wiki/Puntland_counter-terrorism_operations "Puntland counter-terrorism operations")
      * At least three [IS–Somalia](/wiki/Islamic_State_%E2%80%93_Somalia_Province "Islamic State – Somalia Province") fighters are killed in a joint [Puntland armed forces](/wiki/Puntland_Dervish_Force "Puntland Dervish Force")–[U.S. Africa Command](/wiki/U.S._Africa_Command "U.S. Africa Command") [airstrike](/wiki/Airstrike "Airstrike") targeting IS militants hiding in the [Cal Miskaad](/wiki/Cal_Miskaad "Cal Miskaad") mountains of the [Bari Region](/wiki/Bari_Region "Bari Region") of [Puntland](/wiki/Puntland "Puntland"), [Somalia](/wiki/Somalia "Somalia"). [(Horseed Media)](https://horseedmedia.net/ciidamada-puntland-oo-raadadkii-duqaymaha-ugu-tegey-curaar-oo-ay-maanta-qabsadeen/401255/) [(Hiiraan Online)](https://www.hiiraan.com/news4/2025/Feb/200376/somali_u_s_forces_conduct_airstrike_on_isis_hideout_in_puntland.aspx)
* [Australian frontier wars](/wiki/Australian_frontier_wars "Australian frontier wars")
  + The [University of Newcastle](/wiki/University_of_Newcastle_%28Australia%29 "University of Newcastle (Australia)") publishes the final findings of its eight-year long attempt to record and map all major massacres of [Indigenous Australians](/wiki/Indigenous_Australians "Indigenous Australians") during the [colonisation of Australia](/wiki/History_of_Australia_%281788%E2%80%931850%29 "History of Australia (1788–1850)"), finding that at least 10,000 were killed. [(*The Guardian*)](https://www.theguardian.com/australia-news/2025/feb/23/more-than-10000-first-nations-people-killed-in-australias-frontier-wars-final-massacre-map-shows-ntwnfb)
* [Israeli invasion of Lebanon](/wiki/Israeli_invasion_of_Lebanon_%282024%E2%80%93present%29 "Israeli invasion of Lebanon (2024–present)")
  + [Israel](/wiki/Israel "Israel") launches airstrikes in the [Baalbek](/wiki/Baalbek "Baalbek") area in northeastern [Lebanon](/wiki/Lebanon "Lebanon") and other areas in the south of the country. [(*Times of Israel*)](https://www.timesofisrael.com/liveblog_entry/idf-confirms-hitting-hezbollah-targets-in-fresh-lebanon-airstrikes/)
* [Sudanese civil war](/wiki/Sudanese_civil_war_%282023%E2%80%93present%29 "Sudanese civil war (2023–present)")
  + The [Sudanese Army](/wiki/Sudanese_Armed_Forces "Sudanese Armed Forces") recaptures [El Geteina](/wiki/El_Geteina "El Geteina"), [White Nile State](/wiki/White_Nile_State "White Nile State"), [Sudan](/wiki/Sudan "Sudan"), after heavy fighting with the [Rapid Support Forces](/wiki/Rapid_Support_Forces "Rapid Support Forces"). [(*Sudan Tribune*)](https://sudantribune.com/article297827/)
* Two toddlers are killed when a [buried land mine](/wiki/Land_mines_in_Cambodia "Land mines in Cambodia") from a [rocket-propelled grenade](/wiki/Rocket-propelled_grenade "Rocket-propelled grenade") that was left from the [Cambodian Civil War](/wiki/Cambodian_Civil_War "Cambodian Civil War") explodes in [Svay Leu District](/wiki/Svay_Leu_District "Svay Leu District"), [Siem Reap province](/wiki/Siem_Reap_province "Siem Reap province"), [Cambodia](/wiki/Cambodia "Cambodia"). [(*Shanghai Daily*)](https://www.shine.cn/news/world/2502231125/)

**Arts and culture**

* [31st Screen Actors Guild Awards](/wiki/31st_Screen_Actors_Guild_Awards "31st Screen Actors Guild Awards")
  + At the annual [Screen Actors Guild Awards](/wiki/Screen_Actors_Guild_Awards "Screen Actors Guild Awards"), [Timothée Chalamet](/wiki/Timoth%C3%A9e_Chalamet "Timothée Chalamet") wins [Outstanding Leading Male Performance](/wiki/Screen_Actors_Guild_Award_for_Outstanding_Performance_by_a_Male_Actor_in_a_Leading_Role "Screen Actors Guild Award for Outstanding Performance by a Male Actor in a Leading Role") for his role as [Bob Dylan](/wiki/Bob_Dylan "Bob Dylan") in *[A Complete Unknown](/wiki/A_Complete_Unknown "A Complete Unknown")*, while [Demi Moore](/wiki/Demi_Moore "Demi Moore") wins [Outstanding Leading Female Performance](/wiki/Screen_Actors_Guild_Award_for_Outstanding_Performance_by_a_Female_Actor_in_a_Leading_Role "Screen Actors Guild Award for Outstanding Performance by a Female Actor in a Leading Role") for her role in *[The Substance](/wiki/The_Substance "The Substance")*. [Political thriller](/wiki/Political_thriller "Political thriller") film *[Conclave](/wiki/Conclave_%28film%29 "Conclave (film)")* wins [Outstanding Ensemble Performance in a Motion Picture](/wiki/Screen_Actors_Guild_Award_for_Outstanding_Performance_by_a_Cast_in_a_Motion_Picture "Screen Actors Guild Award for Outstanding Performance by a Cast in a Motion Picture"). [(NPR)](https://www.npr.org/2025/02/24/g-s1-50426/conclave-triumphs-at-sag-awards-and-timothee-chalamet-wins-for-best-actor)

**Health and environment**

* [Humanitarian impact of the Sudanese civil war](/wiki/Humanitarian_impact_of_the_Sudanese_civil_war_%282023%E2%80%93present%29 "Humanitarian impact of the Sudanese civil war (2023–present)")
  + Sudanese [officials](/wiki/Government_of_Sudan "Government of Sudan") report that 58 people have been killed and 1,293 people have been affected by a [cholera](/wiki/Cholera "Cholera") outbreak in [Kosti](/wiki/Kosti%2C_Sudan "Kosti, Sudan"), [White Nile State](/wiki/White_Nile_State "White Nile State"). [(AP)](https://apnews.com/article/sudan-cholera-outbreak-south-47ac3f39c10eb549785c7fc24608551a)

**International relations**

* [Peace negotiations in the Russian invasion of Ukraine](/wiki/Peace_negotiations_in_the_Russian_invasion_of_Ukraine "Peace negotiations in the Russian invasion of Ukraine"), [Ukraine–NATO relations](/wiki/Ukraine%E2%80%93NATO_relations "Ukraine–NATO relations")
  + [Ukrainian president](/wiki/President_of_Ukraine "President of Ukraine") [Volodymyr Zelenskyy](/wiki/Volodymyr_Zelenskyy "Volodymyr Zelenskyy") says that he is "ready" to resign from the presidency in exchange for [NATO](/wiki/NATO "NATO") accession as part of a potential peace agreement. [(CNN)](https://www.cnn.com/2025/02/23/europe/ukraine-zelensky-resign-nato-intl/index.html) [(AP)](https://apnews.com/article/russia-ukraine-war-drones-anniversary-putin-trump-c8f73a98d071055be52a1b22b0785ecc)

**Law and crime**

* [American Airlines](/wiki/American_Airlines "American Airlines") Flight 292, flying from [New York](/wiki/John_F._Kennedy_International_Airport "John F. Kennedy International Airport"), [United States](/wiki/United_States "United States"), to [New Delhi](/wiki/Indira_Gandhi_International_Airport "Indira Gandhi International Airport"), [India](/wiki/India "India"), is forced to divert to [Rome Fiumicino Airport](/wiki/Rome_Fiumicino_Airport "Rome Fiumicino Airport") in [Rome](/wiki/Rome "Rome"), [Italy](/wiki/Italy "Italy"), due to an unspecified security concern later deemed to be non-credible. The flight was over the [Caspian Sea](/wiki/Caspian_Sea "Caspian Sea") near [Turkmenistan](/wiki/Turkmenistan "Turkmenistan") when it diverted back towards [Europe](/wiki/Europe "Europe"). [(AP)](https://apnews.com/article/italy-us-india-flight-diversion-6738435dd6f4dd8d6249dc5d30452610)

**Politics and elections**

* [2025 German federal election](/wiki/2025_German_federal_election "2025 German federal election")
  + [Germans](/wiki/Germans "Germans") vote to elect the [Bundestag](/wiki/Bundestag "Bundestag"). The opposition [CDU/CSU](/wiki/CDU/CSU "CDU/CSU") wins a [plurality](/wiki/Plurality_%28voting%29 "Plurality (voting)"), with 28.5% of the vote and 208 seats. The governing [Social Democratic Party](/wiki/Social_Democratic_Party_of_Germany "Social Democratic Party of Germany") finishes in third place with 16.4% and 120 seats, while the [far-right](/wiki/Far-right_politics_in_Germany_%281945%E2%80%93present%29 "Far-right politics in Germany (1945–present)") [Alternative for Germany](/wiki/Alternative_for_Germany "Alternative for Germany") finishes in second place with 20.8% and 152 seats. [(CNN)](https://www.cnn.com/2025/02/23/europe/german-election-results-cdu-afd-intl/index.html) [(DW)](https://www.dw.com/en/german-election-friedrich-merz-urges-independence-from-us/live-71700729)
* [Funeral of Hassan Nasrallah and Hashem Safieddine](/wiki/Funeral_of_Hassan_Nasrallah "Funeral of Hassan Nasrallah")
  + The joint funeral for [Hezbollah](/wiki/Hezbollah "Hezbollah") leaders [Hassan Nasrallah](/wiki/Hassan_Nasrallah "Hassan Nasrallah") and [Hashem Safieddine](/wiki/Hashem_Safieddine "Hashem Safieddine") is held at the [Camille Chamoun Sports City Stadium](/wiki/Camille_Chamoun_Sports_City_Stadium "Camille Chamoun Sports City Stadium") in [Beirut](/wiki/Beirut "Beirut"), [Lebanon](/wiki/Lebanon "Lebanon"). [(AP)](https://apnews.com/article/lebanon-israel-hezbollah-funeral-nasrallah-hashem-safieddine-5b698c1d403887135e35b20c4cb22413)
* [Protests against the Russian invasion of Ukraine](/wiki/Protests_against_the_Russian_invasion_of_Ukraine "Protests against the Russian invasion of Ukraine")
  + Protests are held across [Europe](/wiki/Europe "Europe") and [Canada](/wiki/Canada "Canada") to mark the 3rd year anniversary of the [Russian invasion of Ukraine](/wiki/Russian_invasion_of_Ukraine "Russian invasion of Ukraine"). [(*Kyiv Independent*)](https://kyivindependent.com/thousands-rally-across-europe-canada-ahead-of-3rd-anniversary-of-russias-full-scale-invasion/)
* The [Vatican](/wiki/Holy_See "Holy See") announces that [Pope Francis](/wiki/Pope_Francis "Pope Francis") remains in critical condition, with a new diagnosis of mild [kidney failure](/wiki/Kidney_failure "Kidney failure"), along with pre-existing conditions [pneumonia](/wiki/Pneumonia "Pneumonia") and other unidentified [respiratory diseases](/wiki/Respiratory_disease "Respiratory disease"). [(AP)](https://apnews.com/article/vatican-pope-pneumonia-06324d49846f26a24acec1da5fc74ab2)

**Sports**

* In [cricket](/wiki/Cricket "Cricket") under the [ODI format](/wiki/One_Day_International "One Day International"), [Indian](/wiki/Cricket_in_India "Cricket in India") cricketer [Virat Kohli](/wiki/Virat_Kohli "Virat Kohli") becomes the first player to reach the 51 [centuries](/wiki/Century_%28cricket%29 "Century (cricket)") and the fastest player to reach 14,000 [runs](/wiki/Run_%28cricket%29 "Run (cricket)"). [(*Times of India*)](https://timesofindia.indiatimes.com/sports/cricket/icc-champions-trophy-2025/champions-trophy-2025-virat-kohli-leads-the-charge-as-india-demolish-pakistan-in-one-sided-affair/articleshow/118509034.cms) [(AP)](https://apnews.com/article/kohli-champions-trophy-fastest-14000-runs-record-2b390d8ada093df935cca708df133563)

February 24, 2025 (2025-02-24) (Monday)

* [edit](https://en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Portal:Current_events/2025_February_24&action=edit&editintro=Portal:Current_events/Edit_instructions)
* [history](https://en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Portal:Current_events/2025_February_24&action=history)
* [watch](https://en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Portal:Current_events/2025_February_24&action=watch)

**Armed conflicts and attacks**

* [War against the Islamic State](/wiki/War_against_the_Islamic_State "War against the Islamic State")
  + [Islamic State insurgency in Puntland](/wiki/Islamic_State_insurgency_in_Puntland "Islamic State insurgency in Puntland")
    - [Puntland counter-terrorism operations](/wiki/Puntland_counter-terrorism_operations "Puntland counter-terrorism operations")
      * [Puntland forces](/wiki/Puntland_Dervish_Force "Puntland Dervish Force") capture key locations, including Dararmadobe, Uraar and the Four Corners of Mountains in Gaatir Oodan, which have served as command and defense bases for the [Islamic State militias](/wiki/Islamic_State_%E2%80%93_Somalia_Province "Islamic State – Somalia Province"). Troops uncover mass graves, including the bodies of senior Middle East [ISIL](/wiki/ISIL "ISIL") members killed in [UAE](/wiki/United_Arab_Emirates_Air_Force "United Arab Emirates Air Force") and [US airstrikes](/wiki/American_military_intervention_in_Somalia_%282007%E2%80%93present%29 "American military intervention in Somalia (2007–present)"). Vehicles and motorbikes rigged with explosives were found in the [Cal Miskaad](/wiki/Cal_Miskaad "Cal Miskaad") mountains of [Puntland’s](/wiki/Puntland "Puntland") [Bari Region](/wiki/Bari_Region "Bari Region"). [(Garowe Online)](https://www.garoweonline.com/en/news/puntland/somalia-mass-graves-discovered-in-puntland-as-isis-lose-grounds) [(Hiiraan Online)](https://www.hiiraan.com/news4/2025/Feb/200395/puntland_forces_capture_key_isis_strongholds_in_al_miskaat_mountains.aspx)
* [Russian invasion of Ukraine](/wiki/Russian_invasion_of_Ukraine "Russian invasion of Ukraine")
  + [Attacks in Russia during the Russian invasion of Ukraine](/wiki/Attacks_in_Russia_during_the_Russian_invasion_of_Ukraine "Attacks in Russia during the Russian invasion of Ukraine")
    - The [Ryazan Refinery](/wiki/Ryazan_Refinery "Ryazan Refinery") in [Ryazan](/wiki/Ryazan "Ryazan"), [Russia](/wiki/Russia "Russia"), suspends operations after an overnight [drone attack](/wiki/Drone_warfare "Drone warfare") by [Ukraine](/wiki/Ukraine "Ukraine") destroys the main [crude distillation unit](/wiki/Atmospheric_distillation_of_crude_oil#atmopsheric_crude_distillation_unit "Atmospheric distillation of crude oil") at the facility. Locals report hearing at least five explosions during the attack. [(Reuters)](https://www.reuters.com/world/europe/russias-ryazan-oil-refinery-halts-operations-after-drone-strike-sources-say-2025-02-24/)
* [Syrian civil war](/wiki/Syrian_civil_war "Syrian civil war")
  + [Sectarianism and minorities in the Syrian civil war](/wiki/Sectarianism_and_minorities_in_the_Syrian_civil_war "Sectarianism and minorities in the Syrian civil war")
    - [Druze](/wiki/Druze "Druze") militia leaders announce the formation of the [Suwayda Military Council](/wiki/Suwayda_Military_Council "Suwayda Military Council") as a coalition of [southern Syrian forces](/wiki/Southern_Syria "Southern Syria") for promoting regional [secularism](/wiki/Secularism "Secularism") and [democracy](/wiki/Democracy "Democracy"). The council accuses the [Syrian transitional government](/wiki/First_Syrian_transitional_government "First Syrian transitional government") of committing [ethnic cleansing](/wiki/Ethnic_cleansing "Ethnic cleansing") operations and [extrajudicial killings](/wiki/Extrajudicial_killing "Extrajudicial killing"), and vows to prevent [Syrian Armed Forces](/wiki/Syrian_Armed_Forces "Syrian Armed Forces") from entering [Druze settlements](/wiki/Druze_in_Syria "Druze in Syria"). [(El Manshar)](https://elmanshar.com/2025/02/24/%D8%A7%D9%84%D9%85%D8%AC%D9%84%D8%B3-%D8%A7%D9%84%D8%B9%D8%B3%D9%83%D8%B1%D9%8A-%D9%81%D9%8A-%D8%A7%D9%84%D8%B3%D9%88%D9%8A%D8%AF%D8%A7%D8%A1-%D9%8A%D8%B9%D9%84%D9%86-%D8%A7%D9%86%D8%B7%D9%84%D8%A7/) [(El Manshar 2)](https://elmanshar.com/2025/02/23/%D8%AA%D8%B4%D9%83%D9%8A%D9%84-%D8%A7%D9%84%D9%85%D8%AC%D9%84%D8%B3-%D8%A7%D9%84%D8%B9%D8%B3%D9%83%D8%B1%D9%8A-%D9%81%D9%8A-%D8%A7%D9%84%D8%B3%D9%88%D9%8A%D8%AF%D8%A7%D8%A1-%D8%AF%D8%B1%D9%88%D8%B2/)
* [2020s European re-armament](/wiki/2020s_European_re-armament "2020s European re-armament")
  + [German chancellor-in-waiting](/wiki/Chancellor_of_Germany "Chancellor of Germany") [Friedrich Merz](/wiki/Friedrich_Merz "Friedrich Merz") declares the rapid re-[militarization](/wiki/Militarization "Militarization") of [Germany](/wiki/Germany "Germany") and [Europe](/wiki/Europe "Europe") as a whole to be an immediate priority, in order to provide [military support](/wiki/List_of_military_aid_to_Ukraine_during_the_Russo-Ukrainian_War "List of military aid to Ukraine during the Russo-Ukrainian War") for [Ukraine](/wiki/Ukraine "Ukraine") against [Russia](/wiki/Russia "Russia"), as well as to pursue European military independence from the [United States](/wiki/United_States "United States") and possibly [NATO](/wiki/NATO "NATO"). [(BBC News)](https://www.bbc.com/news/articles/cpv4n0dg3v3o)
* [Terrorism in France](/wiki/Terrorism_in_France "Terrorism in France")
  + Three [molotov cocktails](/wiki/Molotov_cocktail "Molotov cocktail") are thrown at the [Russian consulate](/wiki/List_of_diplomatic_missions_of_Russia "List of diplomatic missions of Russia") in [Marseille](/wiki/Marseille "Marseille"), [France](/wiki/France "France"). No perpetrators are apprehended, but [police](/wiki/National_Police_%28France%29 "National Police (France)") suspect [terrorism](/wiki/Terrorism "Terrorism"). [(France24)](https://www.france24.com/en/europe/20250224-russia-demands-investigation-into-explosions-heard-at-marseille-consulate)

**Business and economy**

* American [coffeehouse](/wiki/Coffeehouse "Coffeehouse") chain [Starbucks](/wiki/Starbucks "Starbucks") announces that it is cutting 1,100 jobs across its stores in the [United States](/wiki/United_States "United States") as part of [cost reduction](/wiki/Cost_reduction "Cost reduction") measures. The company also announces that its menu will be "simplified" and shrunk by 33%. [(BBC News)](https://www.bbc.co.uk/news/articles/c3rnq2lv1lzo)

**Health and environment**

* [Health in the Democratic Republic of the Congo](/wiki/Health_in_the_Democratic_Republic_of_the_Congo "Health in the Democratic Republic of the Congo")
  + Over 50 people die after [an unknown virus outbreak](/wiki/2025_Equateur_disease_outbreak "2025 Equateur disease outbreak") in northwestern [Democratic Republic of the Congo](/wiki/Democratic_Republic_of_the_Congo "Democratic Republic of the Congo"). [(CTV News)](https://www.ctvnews.ca/world/article/an-unknown-illness-kills-over-50-people-in-part-of-congo-with-hours-between-symptoms-and-death/)
* [Measles resurgence in the United States](/wiki/Measles_resurgence_in_the_United_States "Measles resurgence in the United States")
  + The [Department of State Health Services](/wiki/Texas_Department_of_State_Health_Services "Texas Department of State Health Services") in [Texas](/wiki/Texas "Texas"), [United States](/wiki/United_States "United States"), places several major cities in the state on high alert due to a [measles](/wiki/Measles "Measles") outbreak that spreads to 99 people in Texas and [New Mexico](/wiki/New_Mexico "New Mexico"), the third-largest [outbreak](/wiki/Disease_outbreak "Disease outbreak") since it was considered [eliminated](/wiki/Eradication_of_infectious_diseases#Measles "Eradication of infectious diseases") in the U.S. in 2000. [(Texas Public Radio)](https://www.tpr.org/public-health/2025-02-23/breaking-news-possible-measles-exposures-in-san-antonio) [(*The Independent*)](https://www.independent.co.uk/news/health/texas-measles-outbreak-symptoms-vaccine-b2703631.html)

**International relations**

* [Peace negotiations in the Russian invasion of Ukraine](/wiki/Peace_negotiations_in_the_Russian_invasion_of_Ukraine "Peace negotiations in the Russian invasion of Ukraine")
  + The [United Nations](/wiki/United_Nations "United Nations") [General Assembly](/wiki/UN_General_Assembly "UN General Assembly") votes 93–18, with 65 [abstentions](/wiki/Abstention "Abstention"), to pass a resolution condemning Russia’s [war](/wiki/Russian_invasion_of_Ukraine "Russian invasion of Ukraine") against Ukraine. The 18 countries that voted against include the [United States](/wiki/United_States "United States"), [Russia](/wiki/Russia "Russia"), [Israel](/wiki/Israel "Israel"), [Belarus](/wiki/Belarus "Belarus"), and [North Korea](/wiki/North_Korea "North Korea"). [(CNN)](https://amp.cnn.com/cnn/2025/02/24/politics/us-joins-russia-ukraine-un-vote) [(NPR)](https://www.npr.org/2025/02/24/g-s1-50473/un-ukraine-resolution-russia)

**Law and crime**

* The [Australian](/wiki/Australia "Australia") [eSafety Commission](/wiki/Australian_Communications_and_Media_Authority "Australian Communications and Media Authority") fines [instant messaging](/wiki/Instant_messaging "Instant messaging") service [Telegram](/wiki/Telegram_%28software%29 "Telegram (software)") [A$](/wiki/Australian_dollar "Australian dollar")1 million ([US$](/wiki/United_States_dollar "United States dollar")640,000) for delaying its response to inquiries on preventing [child exploitation](/wiki/Online_child_abuse "Online child abuse") and [extremist](/wiki/Online_youth_radicalization "Online youth radicalization") content. [(Reuters)](https://www.reuters.com/world/asia-pacific/australia-fines-telegram-delay-answering-child-abuse-terror-questions-2025-02-23/)

**Science and technology**

* [NASA](/wiki/NASA "NASA") formally announces that [asteroid](/wiki/Asteroid "Asteroid") [2024 YR4](/wiki/2024_YR4 "2024 YR4") now poses "no significant threat" to [Earth](/wiki/Earth "Earth") in [2032](/wiki/2032 "2032") and beyond as the chances of an impact drop to 1-in-59,000 (0.0017%). This means a [planetary defense](/wiki/Asteroid_impact_avoidance "Asteroid impact avoidance") mission to intercept and deflect the object in 2028 during a [close flyby](/wiki/Flyby_%28spaceflight%29 "Flyby (spaceflight)") of Earth is no longer necessary. [(NASA)](https://blogs.nasa.gov/planetarydefense/2025/02/24/latest-calculations-conclude-asteroid-2024-yr4-now-poses-no-significant-threat-to-earth-in-2032-and-beyond/) [(Ars Technica)](https://arstechnica.com/space/2025/02/asteroid-2024-yr4-may-be-a-dud-but-we-will-soon-find-many-more-threats/)

February 25, 2025 (2025-02-25) (Tuesday)

* [edit](https://en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Portal:Current_events/2025_February_25&action=edit&editintro=Portal:Current_events/Edit_instructions)
* [history](https://en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Portal:Current_events/2025_February_25&action=history)
* [watch](https://en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Portal:Current_events/2025_February_25&action=watch)

**Armed conflicts and attacks**

* [Kivu conflict](/wiki/Kivu_conflict "Kivu conflict")
  + [M23 campaign](/wiki/M23_campaign_%282022%E2%80%93present%29 "M23 campaign (2022–present)")
    - [2025 Uvira offensive](/wiki/2025_Uvira_offensive "2025 Uvira offensive")
      * The [Congolese military](/wiki/Armed_Forces_of_the_Democratic_Republic_of_the_Congo "Armed Forces of the Democratic Republic of the Congo") launches an attack against [M23](/wiki/March_23_Movement "March 23 Movement")-aligned rebels around the town of [Minembwe](/wiki/Minembwe "Minembwe") in [South Kivu](/wiki/South_Kivu "South Kivu") in an effort to recapture it, and claims to have killed four rebel commanders in a drone strike. [(Critical Threats Project)](https://www.criticalthreats.org/briefs/congo-war-security-review/congo-war-security-review-february-25-2025)
* [Syrian civil war](/wiki/Syrian_civil_war "Syrian civil war")
  + [Israeli invasion of Syria](/wiki/Israeli_invasion_of_Syria_%282024%E2%80%93present%29 "Israeli invasion of Syria (2024–present)")
    - The [Israeli Air Force](/wiki/Israeli_Air_Force "Israeli Air Force") strikes targets throughout [Southern Syria](/wiki/Southern_Syria "Southern Syria") as [Israel](/wiki/Israel "Israel") begins a [military operation](/wiki/Military_operation "Military operation") to "demilitarize" the southern Syrian governorates of [Daraa](/wiki/Daraa_Governorate "Daraa Governorate"), [Suwayda](/wiki/Suwayda_Governorate "Suwayda Governorate") and [Quneitra](/wiki/Quneitra_Governorate "Quneitra Governorate"). Syrian [state media](/wiki/State_media "State media") reports [airstrikes](/wiki/Airstrike "Airstrike") near [Damascus](/wiki/Damascus "Damascus"). At least two people are reportedly killed. [(ABC News)](https://abcnews.go.com/International/israel-conducting-strikes-southern-syria/story?id=119183725) [(*The Times of India*)](https://timesofindia.indiatimes.com/world/middle-east/israel-strikes-military-targets-in-southern-syria-two-killed/articleshow/118569022.cms)
* [2020s European re-armament](/wiki/2020s_European_re-armament "2020s European re-armament")
  + The [United Kingdom](/wiki/United_Kingdom "United Kingdom") announces an increase in [military spending](/wiki/Military_budget "Military budget") to 2.5% of its [GDP](/wiki/Gross_domestic_product "Gross domestic product") by [2027](/wiki/2027 "2027"), and 3% by 2034 at the latest. The move comes just before [UK Prime Minister](/wiki/Prime_Minister_of_the_United_Kingdom "Prime Minister of the United Kingdom") [Keir Starmer](/wiki/Keir_Starmer "Keir Starmer") is to meet with [U.S. President](/wiki/President_of_the_United_States "President of the United States") [Donald Trump](/wiki/Donald_Trump "Donald Trump") on Thursday in [Washington, D.C.](/wiki/Washington%2C_D.C. "Washington, D.C.") [(*The New York Times*)](https://www.nytimes.com/2025/02/25/world/europe/uk-defense-spending-starmer.html)
* [Casamance conflict](/wiki/Casamance_conflict "Casamance conflict")
  + The [Senegalese](/wiki/Senegal "Senegal") [government](/wiki/Government_of_Senegal "Government of Senegal") and the [Movement of Democratic Forces of Casamance](/wiki/Movement_of_Democratic_Forces_of_Casamance "Movement of Democratic Forces of Casamance") reach an agreement to end their 40-year conflict at talks mediated by [Bissau-Guinean](/wiki/Guinea-Bissau "Guinea-Bissau") [President](/wiki/President_of_Guinea-Bissau "President of Guinea-Bissau") [Umaro Sissoco Embalo](/wiki/Umaro_Sissoco_Embalo "Umaro Sissoco Embalo"). [(*The Defense Post*)](https://thedefensepost.com/2025/02/25/senegal-casamance-rebels-peace-accord/)
* [Central African Republic Civil War](/wiki/Central_African_Republic_Civil_War "Central African Republic Civil War")
  + Nine people are killed and hundreds of homes are [burned down](/wiki/Arson "Arson") in [3R rebel](/wiki/Return%2C_Reclamation%2C_Rehabilitation "Return, Reclamation, Rehabilitation") attacks in [Bamingui-Bangoran](/wiki/Bamingui-Bangoran "Bamingui-Bangoran"), [Central African Republic](/wiki/Central_African_Republic "Central African Republic"). [(AP)](https://apnews.com/article/central-african-republic-3r-attack-c463bad4ff5e119ce5b355a128f3995b)

**Business and economy**

* American [fabrics](/wiki/Textile_industry "Textile industry") and [handicraft](/wiki/Handicraft "Handicraft") supplies retail chain [Jo-Ann Stores](/wiki/Jo-Ann_Stores "Jo-Ann Stores") files its second [bankruptcy](/wiki/Bankruptcy "Bankruptcy") claim and announces it will close all 800 stores in the 49 [states](/wiki/U.S._state "U.S. state"), with [liquidation sales](/wiki/Closeout_%28sale%29 "Closeout (sale)") beginning immediately. [(NPR)](https://www.npr.org/2025/02/25/nx-s1-5307907/joann-closing-stores-bankruptcy)
* [Iraq](/wiki/Iraq "Iraq") agrees to reopen the [oil pipeline](/wiki/Kirkuk%E2%80%93Ceyhan_Oil_Pipeline "Kirkuk–Ceyhan Oil Pipeline") between [Iraqi Kurdistan](/wiki/Iraqi_Kurdistan "Iraqi Kurdistan") and [Turkey](/wiki/Turkey "Turkey") after a conversation between [U.S. Secretary of State](/wiki/U.S._Secretary_of_State "U.S. Secretary of State") [Marco Rubio](/wiki/Marco_Rubio "Marco Rubio") and [Iraqi Prime Minister](/wiki/Prime_Minister_of_Iraq "Prime Minister of Iraq") [Mohammed Shia' Al Sudani](/wiki/Mohammed_Shia%27_Al_Sudani "Mohammed Shia' Al Sudani"), having been closed for two years due to a dispute between Iraq and Turkey. [(Anadolu Agency)](https://www.aa.com.tr/en/americas/rubio-iraqi-prime-minister-agree-to-reopen-iraq-turkiye-pipeline-state-department/3493471) [(*The Arab Weekly*)](https://thearabweekly.com/rubio-discusses-iraqi-pm-iran-energy-us-business-investments)

**Disasters and accidents**

* [2025 Chile blackout](/wiki/2025_Chile_blackout "2025 Chile blackout")
  + A nationwide [power outage](/wiki/Power_outage "Power outage") occurs in [Chile](/wiki/Chile "Chile"), impacting most of the country's population and causing the temporary stoppage of several significant industries. [(Reuters)](https://www.reuters.com/world/americas/power-outage-hits-vast-swaths-chile-largest-copper-mine-santiago-streets-2025-02-25/)
* [2025 Queensland floods](/wiki/2025_Queensland_floods "2025 Queensland floods")
  + At least twelve people are killed by a [melioidosis](/wiki/Melioidosis "Melioidosis") outbreak caused by standing waters from persistent [flooding](/wiki/Flood "Flood") in [Queensland](/wiki/Queensland "Queensland"), [Australia](/wiki/Australia "Australia"). [(7News)](https://7news.com.au/news/more-deaths-from-deadly-melioidosis-disease-found-in-flood-water-in-far-north-queensland-c-17844838)
* [2025 Sudanese Air Force Antonov An-26 crash](/wiki/2025_Sudanese_Air_Force_Antonov_An-26_crash "2025 Sudanese Air Force Antonov An-26 crash")
  + A [Sudanese military](/wiki/Sudanese_Armed_Forces "Sudanese Armed Forces") plane crashes shortly after takeoff from [Wadi Seidna Air Base](/wiki/Wadi_Seidna_Air_Base "Wadi Seidna Air Base") on the outskirts of the capital [Khartoum](/wiki/Khartoum "Khartoum"), killing at least 46 people and injuring several others. [(BBC News)](https://www.bbc.com/news/articles/clyn914g249o)
* Four workers are killed and six others are injured when an [elevated highway](/wiki/Elevated_highway "Elevated highway") under construction collapses in [Cheonan](/wiki/Cheonan "Cheonan"), [South Chungcheong Province](/wiki/South_Chungcheong_Province "South Chungcheong Province"), [South Korea](/wiki/South_Korea "South Korea"). [(AP)](https://apnews.com/article/south-korea-elevated-highway-collapse-72744767d151b6ee66eca37397810e0e)
* A [magnitude](/wiki/Richter_scale "Richter scale") 5.9 [earthquake](/wiki/Earthquake "Earthquake") hits near the [Dominican Republic](/wiki/Dominican_Republic "Dominican Republic") and [Puerto Rico](/wiki/Puerto_Rico "Puerto Rico"), with no damage reported. [(ABC News)](https://abcnews.go.com/amp/International/wireStory/59-magnitude-quake-strikes-dominican-republic-puerto-rico-119157309)

**International relations**

* [Rwanda–United Kingdom relations](/wiki/Rwanda%E2%80%93United_Kingdom_relations "Rwanda–United Kingdom relations"), [Democratic Republic of the Congo–Rwanda conflict](/wiki/Democratic_Republic_of_the_Congo%E2%80%93Rwanda_conflict "Democratic Republic of the Congo–Rwanda conflict")
  + The [UK government](/wiki/Government_of_the_United_Kingdom "Government of the United Kingdom") suspends financial aid and imposes economic sanctions on several high-ranking [Rwandan](/wiki/Rwanda "Rwanda") officials over the country's military support for [M23 rebels](/wiki/March_23_Movement "March 23 Movement") in the [Democratic Republic of the Congo](/wiki/Democratic_Republic_of_the_Congo "Democratic Republic of the Congo"). [(Reuters)](https://www.reuters.com/world/africa/uk-pause-bilateral-aid-rwanda-over-congo-conflict-2025-02-25/)
* [Ukraine–United States relations](/wiki/Ukraine%E2%80%93United_States_relations "Ukraine–United States relations")
  + [Ukrainian Justice Minister](/wiki/Ministry_of_Justice_%28Ukraine%29 "Ministry of Justice (Ukraine)") [Olha Stefanishyna](/wiki/Olha_Stefanishyna "Olha Stefanishyna") announces that [Ukraine](/wiki/Ukraine "Ukraine") has reached a deal with the [United States](/wiki/United_States "United States") on mineral resources. [(Kyiv Independent)](https://kyivindependent.com/breaking-kyiv-washington-reach-agreement-on-minerals-deal/)

**Law and crime**

* [2025 Thiruvananthapuram mass murder](/w/index.php?title=2025_Thiruvananthapuram_mass_murder&action=edit&redlink=1 "2025 Thiruvananthapuram mass murder (page does not exist)")
  + A man brutally beat ( five people, including his brother, girlfriend, to death with a hammer in [Thiruvananthapuram](/wiki/Thiruvananthapuram "Thiruvananthapuram"), [Kerala](/wiki/Kerala "Kerala"), South India. [gulfnews](https://gulfnews.com/world/asia/india/kerala-horror-23-year-old-kills-six-including-girlfriend-and-brother-surrenders-to-police-1.500045264) [Economic Times](https://economictimes.indiatimes.com/news/new-updates/kerala-mass-murder-23-year-old-man-goes-house-to-house-killing-5-including-teen-brother-and-girlfriend-shocking-details-emerge/articleshow/118573876.cms?from=mdr)
* [Environmental issues in Brazil](/wiki/Environmental_issues_in_Brazil "Environmental issues in Brazil")
  + The [Brazilian](/wiki/Brazil "Brazil") [Public Prosecutor's Office](/wiki/Public_Prosecutor%27s_Office_%28Brazil%29 "Public Prosecutor's Office (Brazil)") files a lawsuit against [mining](/wiki/Mining "Mining") corporation [Vale S.A.](/wiki/Vale_S.A. "Vale S.A.") and the state of [Pará](/wiki/Par%C3%A1 "Pará") for mass [metal poisoning](/wiki/Metal_poisoning "Metal poisoning") that has affected the [Xikrin](/wiki/Kayapo "Kayapo") [indigenous people](/wiki/Indigenous_peoples_of_Brazil "Indigenous peoples of Brazil"), whose [Indigenous Territory](/wiki/Kayap%C3%B3_Indigenous_Territory "Kayapó Indigenous Territory") is located in the state. [(News-Press NOW)](https://www.newspressnow.com/news/world_news/in-brazil-mining-giant-vale-is-sued-over-metal-contamination-found-in-indigenous-peoples/article_9b5bfe1d-2832-5228-bcc6-9cf96adcb615.html)
* The [Indonesian](/wiki/Indonesia "Indonesia") [Attorney General’s Office](/wiki/Attorney_General%27s_Office_of_Indonesia "Attorney General's Office of Indonesia") arrests three executives of state-owned oil and gas company [Pertamina](/wiki/Pertamina "Pertamina") on charges of corruption and fraud regarding gasoline quality that cost the government more than $11 billion [USD](/wiki/United_States_dollar "United States dollar"). [(*The Straits Times*)](https://www.straitstimes.com/asia/se-asia/indonesian-prosecutors-arrest-three-pertamina-unit-executives-over-oil-imports) [(*The Jakarta Globe*)](https://jakartaglobe.id/news/pertamina-vows-cooperation-as-executives-named-in-119b-corruption-scandal)

**Politics and elections**

* [Second presidency of Donald Trump](/wiki/Second_presidency_of_Donald_Trump "Second presidency of Donald Trump")
  + [Executive orders in the second presidency of Donald Trump](/wiki/List_of_executive_orders_in_the_second_presidency_of_Donald_Trump "List of executive orders in the second presidency of Donald Trump")
    - [U.S. District Judge](/wiki/United_States_federal_judge "United States federal judge") for the [Western Washington District Court](/wiki/United_States_District_Court_for_the_Western_District_of_Washington "United States District Court for the Western District of Washington") [Jamal Whitehead](/wiki/Jamal_Whitehead "Jamal Whitehead") temporarily blocks [President](/wiki/President_of_the_United_States "President of the United States") [Donald Trump](/wiki/Donald_Trump "Donald Trump")'s [executive order](/wiki/Executive_order "Executive order") to suspend the [Refugee Admissions Program](/wiki/United_States_Refugee_Admissions_Program "United States Refugee Admissions Program"), ruling that President Trump cannot nullify the law passed by [Congress](/wiki/United_States_Congress "United States Congress"), following a [lawsuit](/wiki/Lawsuit "Lawsuit") against the [Trump administration](/wiki/Second_presidency_of_Donald_Trump "Second presidency of Donald Trump") by the [International Refugee Assistance Project](/wiki/International_Refugee_Assistance_Project "International Refugee Assistance Project"). [(AP)](https://apnews.com/article/trump-refugee-seattle-ruling-lawsuit-eef485154e2a3f008a01d6790ce0ee06)

February 26, 2025 (2025-02-26) (Wednesday)

* [edit](https://en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Portal:Current_events/2025_February_26&action=edit&editintro=Portal:Current_events/Edit_instructions)
* [history](https://en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Portal:Current_events/2025_February_26&action=history)
* [watch](https://en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Portal:Current_events/2025_February_26&action=watch)

**Armed conflicts and attacks**

* [Somali Civil War](/wiki/Somali_Civil_War_%282009%E2%80%93present%29 "Somali Civil War (2009–present)")
  + [African Union Support and Stabilization Mission in Somalia](/wiki/African_Union_Support_and_Stabilization_Mission_in_Somalia "African Union Support and Stabilization Mission in Somalia")
    - The [Somalian](/wiki/Somalia "Somalia") [government](/wiki/Government_of_Somalia "Government of Somalia") and the [African Union](/wiki/African_Union "African Union") finalize the troop distribution for the new [peacekeeping](/wiki/Peacekeeping "Peacekeeping") mission [AUSSOM](/wiki/African_Union_Support_and_Stabilization_Mission_in_Somalia "African Union Support and Stabilization Mission in Somalia"), resolving prior disputes with [Ethiopia](/wiki/Ethiopian%E2%80%93Somali_conflict "Ethiopian–Somali conflict") and later [Burundi](/wiki/Burundi_National_Defence_Force "Burundi National Defence Force"). The mission will deploy 11,900 personnel, including [soldiers](/wiki/Soldier "Soldier"), [police](/wiki/Police "Police"), and [civilian staff](/wiki/Staff_%28military%29 "Staff (military)"). Under the agreement, [Uganda](/wiki/Uganda "Uganda") will contribute 4,500 troops, followed by [Ethiopia](/wiki/Ethiopia "Ethiopia") with 2,500, [Djibouti](/wiki/Djibouti "Djibouti") with 1,520, [Kenya](/wiki/Kenya "Kenya") with 1,410, and [Egypt](/wiki/Egypt "Egypt") with 1,091. [(VOA)](https://www.voanews.com/a/au-somalia-agree-on-troop-numbers-for-new-mission/7987913.html)
* [Sudanese civil war](/wiki/Sudanese_civil_war_%282023%E2%80%93present%29 "Sudanese civil war (2023–present)"), [2024 famine in Sudan](/wiki/2024_famine_in_Sudan "2024 famine in Sudan")
  + The [United Nations](/wiki/United_Nations "United Nations")-operated [World Food Programme](/wiki/World_Food_Programme "World Food Programme") announces it has been forced to temporarily cease the distribution of [humanitarian aid](/wiki/Humanitarian_aid "Humanitarian aid") in the [Zamzam refugee camp](/wiki/Zamzam_refugee_camp "Zamzam refugee camp") in [North Darfur](/wiki/North_Darfur "North Darfur"), [Sudan](/wiki/Sudan "Sudan"), due to an [escalation in fighting](/wiki/Conflict_escalation "Conflict escalation") between the [Sudanese Armed Forces](/wiki/Sudanese_Armed_Forces "Sudanese Armed Forces") and the [Rapid Support Forces](/wiki/Rapid_Support_Forces "Rapid Support Forces") in the region. [Doctors Without Borders](/wiki/Doctors_Without_Borders "Doctors Without Borders") also temporarily ceased operations in the camp last week. [(DW)](https://www.dw.com/en/sudan-un-food-agency-pauses-aid-in-famine-hit-refugee-camp/a-71763311)
* [Mexican drug war](/wiki/Mexican_drug_war "Mexican drug war")
  + A [roadside bombing](/wiki/Improvised_explosive_device "Improvised explosive device") kills a [Texan](/wiki/Texas "Texas") rancher in [San Fernando, Tamaulipas](/wiki/San_Fernando%2C_Tamaulipas "San Fernando, Tamaulipas"), [Mexico](/wiki/Mexico "Mexico"). Authorities say the victim was driving on his ranch when the explosive device detonated. [(El Financiero)](https://www.elfinanciero.com.mx/border/2025/02/26/ranchero-de-texas-muere-por-explosivo-en-tamaulipas-advierten-que-carteles-amenazan-la-frontera/)

**Arts and culture**

* [Conservation and restoration of Pompeian frescoes](/wiki/Conservation_and_restoration_of_Pompeian_frescoes "Conservation and restoration of Pompeian frescoes")
  + Archeologists find monumental [frescoes](/wiki/Fresco "Fresco") at the [House of Thiasus](/wiki/House_of_Thiasus "House of Thiasus") in [Pompeii](/wiki/Pompeii "Pompeii"), [Campania](/wiki/Campania "Campania"), [Italy](/wiki/Italy "Italy"), providing insight into the [Dionysian Mysteries](/wiki/Dionysian_Mysteries "Dionysian Mysteries"). [(Reuters)](https://www.reuters.com/world/europe/rare-frescoes-unearthed-pompeii-shed-light-ancient-rituals-2025-02-26/)

**Business and economy**

* [2025 United States tariffs against the European Union](/wiki/2025_United_States_tariffs_against_the_European_Union "2025 United States tariffs against the European Union")
  + [United States President](/wiki/President_of_the_United_States "President of the United States") [Donald Trump](/wiki/Donald_Trump "Donald Trump") announces impending 25% [tariffs](/wiki/Tariff "Tariff") on the [European Union](/wiki/European_Union "European Union"), which he states will be generally applied to sectors such as the [automotive industry](/wiki/Automotive_industry "Automotive industry"). [(*The Guardian*)](https://www.theguardian.com/us-news/2025/feb/26/trump-european-union-tariffs)
* British [oil and gas](/wiki/Petroleum_industry "Petroleum industry") company [BP](/wiki/BP "BP") announces an agreement with the [Iraqi](/wiki/Iraq "Iraq") [government](/wiki/Government_of_Iraq "Government of Iraq") to develop four [oil fields](/wiki/Oil_field "Oil field") around [Kirkuk](/wiki/Kirkuk "Kirkuk") and increase production, with the value of BP's investment estimated at US$25 billion. [(Society of Petroleum Engineers)](https://jpt.spe.org/bp-signs-deal-to-rehab-iraqs-kirkuk-oil-assets-boost-production) [(Reuters)](https://www.reuters.com/business/energy/iraq-bp-agree-develop-four-kirkuk-fields-iraqi-state-news-reports-2025-02-25/)

**Disasters and accidents**

* Eighteen people are killed and thirty-one others are injured when a bus overturns in [Prachinburi province](/wiki/Prachinburi_province "Prachinburi province"), [Thailand](/wiki/Thailand "Thailand"). [(CTV News)](https://www.ctvnews.ca/world/article/18-dead-in-a-bus-crash-in-eastern-thailand/)

**Health and environment**

* An [unvaccinated](/wiki/Vaccine_hesitancy "Vaccine hesitancy") child dies of [measles](/wiki/Measles "Measles") at a hospital in [Lubbock](/wiki/Lubbock "Lubbock"), [Texas](/wiki/Texas "Texas"), United States, as the first death since the disease was considered [eradicated](/wiki/Disease_eradication "Disease eradication") in the country in 2000. [(ABC News)](https://abcnews.go.com/Health/1st-measles-death-linked-outbreak-texas-confirmed-child/story?id=119208967) [(AP)](https://apnews.com/article/measles-outbreak-west-texas-death-rfk-41adc66641e4a56ce2b2677480031ab9)

**International relations**

* [United States–Venezuela relations](/wiki/United_States%E2%80%93Venezuela_relations "United States–Venezuela relations")
  + U.S. President [Donald Trump](/wiki/Donald_Trump "Donald Trump") cancels [energy](/wiki/Energy_industry "Energy industry") corporation [Chevron](/wiki/Chevron_Corporation "Chevron Corporation")'s [license](/wiki/Petroleum_licensing "Petroleum licensing") to operate in [Venezuela](/wiki/Venezuela "Venezuela"). [(Reuters)](https://www.reuters.com/world/americas/trump-orders-termination-oil-deal-with-venezuela-2025-02-26/)
* [United Nations](/wiki/United_Nations "United Nations") [Human Rights Commissioner](/wiki/Office_of_the_United_Nations_High_Commissioner_for_Human_Rights "Office of the United Nations High Commissioner for Human Rights") [Volker Türk](/wiki/Volker_T%C3%BCrk "Volker Türk") condemns [Israel](/wiki/Israel "Israel")'s [human rights](/wiki/Human_rights "Human rights") violations in [Gaza](/wiki/Gaza_Strip "Gaza Strip") and denounces [Israeli settlements](/wiki/Israeli_settlements "Israeli settlements"). [(Reuters)](https://www.reuters.com/world/middle-east/israel-has-shown-unprecedented-disregard-human-rights-gaza-un-human-rights-chief-2025-02-26/)

**Law and crime**

* [2020 Nice stabbing](/wiki/2020_Nice_stabbing "2020 Nice stabbing")
  + [Brahim Aouissaoui](/wiki/2020_Nice_stabbing#Perpetrator "2020 Nice stabbing"), the perpetrator of the 2020 stabbing in [Nice](/wiki/Nice "Nice"), [France](/wiki/France "France"), is sentenced to [life imprisonment](/wiki/Life_imprisonment "Life imprisonment") without [parole](/wiki/Parole "Parole"). [(CTV News)](https://www.ctvnews.ca/world/article/a-tunisian-extremist-is-imprisoned-for-life-for-killing-3-people-in-a-french-basilica-in-2020/)
* [2025 Romanian presidential election](/wiki/2025_Romanian_presidential_election "2025 Romanian presidential election")
  + [Călin Georgescu](/wiki/C%C4%83lin_Georgescu "Călin Georgescu"), the candidate received the most votes in the [annulled 2024 presidential election](/wiki/2024_Romanian_presidential_election "2024 Romanian presidential election"), is detained by [police](/wiki/Romanian_Police "Romanian Police") and taken for questioning by the general prosecutor's office over allegations of false statements about financing sources, [illegal possession of weapons](/wiki/Criminal_possession_of_a_weapon "Criminal possession of a weapon"), and forming an organization that is "[fascist](/wiki/Fascist "Fascist"), [racist](/wiki/Racist "Racist"), or [xenophobic](/wiki/Xenophobic "Xenophobic")". [(AP)](https://apnews.com/article/romania-calin-georgescu-528f1875e728f8a789f6622d224303a5)
* [Milorad Dodik](/wiki/Milorad_Dodik "Milorad Dodik"), [President](/wiki/President_of_Republika_Srpska "President of Republika Srpska") of [Republika Srpska](/wiki/Republika_Srpska "Republika Srpska"), an [entity](/wiki/Political_divisions_of_Bosnia_and_Herzegovina "Political divisions of Bosnia and Herzegovina") within [Bosnia and Herzegovina](/wiki/Bosnia_and_Herzegovina "Bosnia and Herzegovina"), is sentenced to one year in prison and banned from participating in politics for six years for "separatist actions", such as advocating for [secession](/wiki/Proposed_secession_of_Republika_Srpska "Proposed secession of Republika Srpska"). [(*The Guardian*)](https://www.theguardian.com/world/2025/feb/26/pro-russia-bosnian-serb-president-milorad-dodik-jailed-for-separatist-actions)

**Politics and elections**

* [2025 Anguillian general election](/wiki/2025_Anguillian_general_election "2025 Anguillian general election")
  + The opposition [Anguilla United Front](/wiki/Anguilla_United_Front "Anguilla United Front") (AUF) wins a majority in the [House of Assembly](/wiki/House_of_Assembly_%28Anguilla%29 "House of Assembly (Anguilla)"). AUF leader [Cora Richardson-Hodge](/wiki/Cora_Richardson-Hodge "Cora Richardson-Hodge") becomes the first female [Premier of Anguilla](/wiki/Premier_of_Anguilla "Premier of Anguilla"). [(*Jamaica Observer*)](https://www.jamaicaobserver.com/2025/02/27/anguillians-elect-first-female-head-government/)
* [Freedom of the press in the United States](/wiki/Freedom_of_the_press_in_the_United_States "Freedom of the press in the United States"), [Gulf of Mexico–America naming dispute](/wiki/Gulf_of_Mexico%E2%80%93America_naming_dispute "Gulf of Mexico–America naming dispute")
  + The [Trump administration](/wiki/Second_presidency_of_Donald_Trump "Second presidency of Donald Trump") bans reporters from the [Associated Press](/wiki/Associated_Press "Associated Press"), [Reuters](/wiki/Reuters "Reuters"), *[Der Tagesspiegel](/wiki/Der_Tagesspiegel "Der Tagesspiegel")*, and *[HuffPost](/wiki/HuffPost "HuffPost")* from the [White House](/wiki/White_House "White House") over their refusal to refer to the [Gulf of Mexico](/wiki/Gulf_of_Mexico "Gulf of Mexico") as the "[Gulf of America](/wiki/Executive_Order_14172 "Executive Order 14172")". [(Reuters)](https://www.reuters.com/world/us/white-house-bars-ap-reuters-other-media-covering-trump-cabinet-meeting-2025-02-26/)
* [Constitutional crisis in Somalia](/wiki/Constitutional_crisis_in_Somalia "Constitutional crisis in Somalia")
  + Somalia's [Federal Parliament](/wiki/Federal_Parliament_of_Somalia "Federal Parliament of Somalia") fails to [meet](/wiki/Meeting_%28parliamentary_procedure%29 "Meeting (parliamentary procedure)") due to a lack of [quorum](/wiki/Quorum "Quorum"), with only 137 [MPs](/wiki/Member_of_parliament "Member of parliament") present, two short of the required amount. The delay raises concerns about a potential [no-confidence motion](/wiki/Motion_of_no_confidence "Motion of no confidence") against [Prime Minister](/wiki/List_of_prime_ministers_of_Somalia "List of prime ministers of Somalia") [Hamza Abdi Barre](/wiki/Hamza_Abdi_Barre "Hamza Abdi Barre")'s [council of ministers](/wiki/Council_of_Ministers_of_Somalia "Council of Ministers of Somalia"). [(Hiiraan Online)](https://www.hiiraan.com/news4/2025/Feb/200428/somali_parliament_fails_to_meet_quorum_fueling_no_confidence_motion_speculation.aspx)

February 27, 2025 (2025-02-27) (Thursday)

* [edit](https://en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Portal:Current_events/2025_February_27&action=edit&editintro=Portal:Current_events/Edit_instructions)
* [history](https://en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Portal:Current_events/2025_February_27&action=history)
* [watch](https://en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Portal:Current_events/2025_February_27&action=watch)

**Armed conflicts and attacks**

* [Israeli–Palestinian conflict](/wiki/Israeli%E2%80%93Palestinian_conflict "Israeli–Palestinian conflict")
  + [Gaza war](/wiki/Gaza_war "Gaza war")
    - [2025 Gaza war ceasefire](/wiki/2025_Gaza_war_ceasefire "2025 Gaza war ceasefire")
      * As part of the first stage of the [ceasefire](/wiki/Ceasefire "Ceasefire") deal, [Hamas](/wiki/Hamas "Hamas") releases the bodies of four [Israeli](/wiki/Israelis "Israelis") [hostages](/wiki/Gaza_war_hostage_crisis "Gaza war hostage crisis") in return for the [Israeli government](/wiki/Israeli_government "Israeli government") releasing 617 [Palestinian](/wiki/Palestinians "Palestinians") [prisoners](/wiki/Palestinian_prisoners_in_Israel "Palestinian prisoners in Israel"). The second phase of the ceasefire has not been negotiated. [(DW)](https://www.dw.com/en/final-swap-of-gaza-truce-deal-sees-return-of-4-dead-hostages/a-71767402)
  + Thirteen people are injured in a [car-ramming attack](/wiki/Vehicle-ramming_attack "Vehicle-ramming attack") in [Pardes Hanna-Karkur](/wiki/Pardes_Hanna-Karkur "Pardes Hanna-Karkur"), [Israel](/wiki/Israel "Israel"). The suspect, a Palestinian residing in [Ma'ale Iron](/wiki/Ma%27ale_Iron "Ma'ale Iron"), is later shot and killed by [police](/wiki/Israel_Police "Israel Police") after an attempted [stabbing](/wiki/Stabbing "Stabbing") attack. [(*Times of Israel*)](https://www.timesofisrael.com/teen-in-critical-condition-after-terror-suspect-plows-car-into-bus-stop-injuring-13/)
* [Kivu conflict](/wiki/Kivu_conflict "Kivu conflict")
  + [2025 Bukavu offensive](/wiki/2025_Bukavu_offensive "2025 Bukavu offensive")
    - [2025 Bukavu M23 rally bombings](/wiki/2025_Bukavu_M23_rally_bombings "2025 Bukavu M23 rally bombings")
      * A [grenade](/wiki/Grenade "Grenade") attack at an [M23](/wiki/March_23_Movement "March 23 Movement") rally in [Bukavu](/wiki/Bukavu "Bukavu"), [Democratic Republic of the Congo](/wiki/Democratic_Republic_of_the_Congo "Democratic Republic of the Congo"), celebrating their recent victory over [government forces](/wiki/Armed_Forces_of_the_Democratic_Republic_of_the_Congo "Armed Forces of the Democratic Republic of the Congo") in the city, kills at least eleven people and wounds 65 others. [(Reuters)](https://www.reuters.com/world/africa/blasts-m23-rally-eastern-congo-kill-11-wound-65-rebel-leader-says-2025-02-27/)
* [Kurdish–Turkish conflict](/wiki/Kurdish%E2%80%93Turkish_conflict "Kurdish–Turkish conflict")
  + [Kurdistan Workers' Party insurgency](/wiki/Kurdistan_Workers%27_Party_insurgency "Kurdistan Workers' Party insurgency")
    - Jailed [Kurdish](/wiki/Kurds "Kurds") leader and [Kurdistan Workers' Party](/wiki/Kurdistan_Workers%27_Party "Kurdistan Workers' Party") (PKK) founder [Abdullah Öcalan](/wiki/Abdullah_%C3%96calan "Abdullah Öcalan") calls for an end to the conflict with [Turkey](/wiki/Turkey "Turkey") and asks the group to disarm and disband, amid peace efforts between the [Turkish government](/wiki/Turkish_government "Turkish government") and the PKK led by the pro-[Kurdish](/wiki/Kurds_in_Turkey "Kurds in Turkey") [Peoples' Equality and Democracy Party](/wiki/Peoples%27_Equality_and_Democracy_Party "Peoples' Equality and Democracy Party"). [(Rudaw)](https://www.rudaw.net/english/middleeast/turkey/27022025) [(Reuters)](https://www.reuters.com/world/middle-east/turkeys-pro-kurdish-party-sets-off-visit-jailed-militant-leader-2025-02-27/) [(DW)](https://www.dw.com/en/turkey-ocalan-calls-for-pkk-to-lay-down-weapons/a-71773113)
* [Somali Civil War](/wiki/Somali_Civil_War_%282009%E2%80%93present%29 "Somali Civil War (2009–present)")
  + [Somali](/wiki/Somalia "Somalia") capital city [Mogadishu](/wiki/Mogadishu "Mogadishu") enters a security lockdown after several [mortars](/wiki/Mortar_%28weapon%29 "Mortar (weapon)") were fired toward [Aden Adde International Airport](/wiki/Aden_Adde_International_Airport "Aden Adde International Airport") during a visit from [Ethiopian Prime Minister](/wiki/Prime_Minister_of_Ethiopia "Prime Minister of Ethiopia") [Abiy Ahmed](/wiki/Abiy_Ahmed "Abiy Ahmed"). [(Anadolu Agency)](http://v.aa.com.tr/3494950)
  + [Somali forces](/wiki/Somali_National_Army "Somali National Army") regain control of [Balad](/wiki/Balad%2C_Somalia "Balad, Somalia") after [Al-Shabaab](/wiki/Al-Shabaab_%28militant_group%29 "Al-Shabaab (militant group)") launches a coordinated attack, detonating [roadside bombs](/wiki/Improvised_explosive_device "Improvised explosive device") and briefly seizing the town. [(Hiiraan Online)](https://www.hiiraan.com/news4/2025/Feb/200443/somali_forces_regain_control_of_bal_ad_after_deadly_al_shabaab_attack.aspx)
