* [Villa Somalia](/wiki/Villa_Somalia "Villa Somalia") security guards open fire on civilians at [Lido Beach](/wiki/Lido_Beach%2C_Mogadishu "Lido Beach, Mogadishu") in Mogadishu while attempting to clear the beach ahead of a visit from Ethiopian Prime Minister Abiy Ahmed, killing a teenage boy and wounding several others. [(Idil News)](https://www.idilnews.com/teenager-shot-dead-as-somali-security-forces-clear-beach-for-ethiopian-pms-visit/) [(HBN)](https://hbnonlinetv.com/khasaare-dhimasho-oo-ka-dhashay-rasaas-lagu-kala-ergayey-dad-shacab-ah-muqdisho/)

**Business and economy**

* [Denmark–United States relations](/wiki/Denmark%E2%80%93United_States_relations "Denmark–United States relations")
  + [Danish](/wiki/Denmark "Denmark") retailer group [Salling Group](/wiki/Salling_Group "Salling Group"), which operates around 34% of the [retail](/wiki/Retail "Retail") [market share](/wiki/Market_share "Market share") in the country, announces it will start differentiating brands owned by [European](/wiki/European_Union "European Union") companies from [American](/wiki/United_States "United States") ones, in retaliation to [U.S. President](/wiki/United_States_President "United States President") [Donald Trump](/wiki/Donald_Trump "Donald Trump")'s [proposed acquisition](/wiki/Proposed_United_States_acquisition_of_Greenland "Proposed United States acquisition of Greenland") of [Greenland](/wiki/Greenland "Greenland"), an [autonomous territory](/wiki/Autonomous_territory "Autonomous territory") of the [Danish Realm](/wiki/Danish_Realm "Danish Realm"). [(DW)](https://www.dw.com/en/danish-grocery-chain-to-distinguish-european-from-us-goods/a-71773488)

**Disasters and accidents**

* A fire at a three-story residential building in [Quezon City](/wiki/Quezon_City "Quezon City"), [Philippines](/wiki/Philippines "Philippines"), kills eight people and injures one other. [(AP)](https://apnews.com/article/philippines-deadly-building-fire-ee49c46908c2d074b5a229faf773b170)
* Two people are killed when a [Robinson R44](/wiki/Robinson_R44 "Robinson R44") helicopter crashes on a private property in [Uvalde](/wiki/Uvalde%2C_Texas "Uvalde, Texas"), [Texas](/wiki/Texas "Texas"), United States. The [Federal Aviation Administration](/wiki/Federal_Aviation_Administration "Federal Aviation Administration") and the [National Transportation Safety Board](/wiki/National_Transportation_Safety_Board "National Transportation Safety Board") are currently investigating the accident. [(KENS-TV)](https://www.kens5.com/video/news/local/texas/latest-details-in-deadly-helicopter-crash-in-kinney-county/273-77d7fde6-3362-4432-a665-e7642e95ffbd)
* Two [Russian](/wiki/Russians "Russians") tourists are killed in a [shark attack](/wiki/Shark_attack "Shark attack") while [scuba diving](/wiki/Scuba_diving "Scuba diving") in the [Verde Island Passage](/wiki/Verde_Island_Passage "Verde Island Passage") off [Batangas](/wiki/Batangas "Batangas"), Philippines. [(Fox News)](https://www.foxnews.com/world/philippines-shark-attack-2-tourists-killed-popular-diving-spot)

**International relations**

* [United Kingdom–United States relations](/wiki/United_Kingdom%E2%80%93United_States_relations "United Kingdom–United States relations")
  + [U.S. President](/wiki/President_of_the_United_States "President of the United States") [Donald Trump](/wiki/Donald_Trump "Donald Trump") meets with [UK Prime Minister](/wiki/Prime_Minister_of_the_United_Kingdom "Prime Minister of the United Kingdom") [Keir Starmer](/wiki/Keir_Starmer "Keir Starmer") in [Washington, D.C.](/wiki/Washington%2C_D.C. "Washington, D.C."), for talks that include the [Russo-Ukrainian War](/wiki/Russo-Ukrainian_War "Russo-Ukrainian War") [peace negotiations](/wiki/Peace_negotiations_in_the_Russian_invasion_of_Ukraine "Peace negotiations in the Russian invasion of Ukraine"). Starmer also presents a letter from [King](/wiki/Monarchy_of_the_United_Kingdom "Monarchy of the United Kingdom") [Charles III](/wiki/Charles_III "Charles III") inviting Trump to visit [London](/wiki/London "London") later this year. [(NPR)](https://www.npr.org/2025/02/27/nx-s1-5310656/trump-keir-starmer-russia-ukraine)

**Law and crime**

* [Persecution of Uyghurs in China](/wiki/Persecution_of_Uyghurs_in_China "Persecution of Uyghurs in China")
  + Forty [Uyghur](/wiki/Uyghurs "Uyghurs") men detained in [Thailand](/wiki/Thailand "Thailand") for over a decade are deported to [China](/wiki/China "China"), despite concerns regarding their persecution. [(Al Arabiya)](https://english.alarabiya.net/News/world/2025/02/27/40-uyghur-men-detained-in-thailand-for-more-than-a-decade-have-been-deported-to-china)
* The [prosecutor's office](/wiki/Tribunal_de_grande_instance_de_Paris "Tribunal de grande instance de Paris") in [Paris](/wiki/Paris "Paris"), [France](/wiki/France "France"), closes a [criminal complaint](/wiki/Complaint "Complaint") case by the [Democratic Republic of the Congo](/wiki/Democratic_Republic_of_the_Congo "Democratic Republic of the Congo") (DRC) against technology company [Apple](/wiki/Apple_%28company%29 "Apple (company)") for alleged [money laundering](/wiki/Money_laundering "Money laundering") and [deceptive business practices](/wiki/Unfair_business_practices "Unfair business practices") related to the purchase of [minerals](/wiki/Illegal_mining "Illegal mining") in the DRC from [armed militias](/wiki/List_of_armed_groups_in_the_Democratic_Republic_of_the_Congo "List of armed groups in the Democratic Republic of the Congo"). It is one of the DRC's two lawsuits, with another in [Belgium](/wiki/Belgium "Belgium"). [(Reuters)](https://www.reuters.com/technology/paris-prosecutor-closes-case-against-apple-over-congo-minerals-document-2025-02-27/)

**Politics and elections**

* [2024 Austrian legislative election](/wiki/2024_Austrian_legislative_election "2024 Austrian legislative election")
  + The [Social Democratic Party](/wiki/Social_Democratic_Party_of_Austria "Social Democratic Party of Austria"), the [Austrian People's Party](/wiki/Austrian_People%27s_Party "Austrian People's Party"), and the [NEOS](/wiki/NEOS_%28Austria%29 "NEOS (Austria)") party in [Austria](/wiki/Austria "Austria") agree to form a [coalition government](/wiki/Coalition_government "Coalition government"), leaving out the [far-right](/wiki/Far-right_politics "Far-right politics") [Freedom Party](/wiki/Freedom_Party_of_Austria "Freedom Party of Austria"), who won the most seats in the [National Council](/wiki/National_Council_%28Austria%29 "National Council (Austria)") in the 2024 legislative election. The coalition agreement ends Austria's longest period without a [government](/wiki/Government_of_Austria "Government of Austria") since [World War II](/wiki/World_War_II "World War II"). [(DW)](https://www.dw.com/en/austria-centrist-parties-form-coalition-without-far-right/a-71765298) [(Euractiv)](https://www.euractiv.com/section/politics/news/austria-centrist-parties-agree-on-coalition-government/)
* The [Trump administration](/wiki/Second_presidency_of_Donald_Trump "Second presidency of Donald Trump") bans [NASA](/wiki/NASA "NASA") scientists and US government officials from attending the UN [Intergovernmental Panel on Climate Change](/wiki/Intergovernmental_Panel_on_Climate_Change "Intergovernmental Panel on Climate Change") conference that started this week in [Hangzhou](/wiki/Hangzhou "Hangzhou"), [China](/wiki/China "China"), which are focused on the seventh [IPCC Assessment Report](/wiki/IPCC_Sixth_Assessment_Report "IPCC Sixth Assessment Report") on [climate change](/wiki/Climate_change "Climate change"). [(*Nature*)](https://www.nature.com/articles/d41586-025-00596-0)

**Science and technology**

* [Meta Platforms](/wiki/Meta_Platforms "Meta Platforms") says it has fixed an error that resulted in [Instagram](/wiki/Instagram "Instagram") users' [Reels](/wiki/Instagram_Reels "Instagram Reels") feeds displaying violent and graphic videos despite these users having [content filters](/wiki/Content_filter "Content filter") enabled. [(Al Arabiya)](https://english.alarabiya.net/News/world/2025/02/27/meta-fixes-error-that-flooded-instagram-reels-with-violent-videos)
* [OpenAI](/wiki/OpenAI "OpenAI") releases their latest large language model, [GPT-4.5](/wiki/GPT-4.5 "GPT-4.5"). [(*The Verge*)](https://www.theverge.com/news/620021/openai-gpt-4-5-orion-ai-model-release)

February 28, 2025 (2025-02-28) (Friday)

* [edit](https://en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Portal:Current_events/2025_February_28&action=edit&editintro=Portal:Current_events/Edit_instructions)
* [history](https://en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Portal:Current_events/2025_February_28&action=history)
* [watch](https://en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Portal:Current_events/2025_February_28&action=watch)

**Attacks and armed conflicts**

* [2025 Darul Uloom Haqqania bombing](/wiki/2025_Darul_Uloom_Haqqania_bombing "2025 Darul Uloom Haqqania bombing")
  + Five people, including [Hamid Ul Haq Haqqani](/wiki/Hamid_Ul_Haq_Haqqani "Hamid Ul Haq Haqqani"), the head of a faction of the [Jamiat Ulema-e-Islam (S)](/wiki/Jamiat_Ulema-e-Islam_%28S%29 "Jamiat Ulema-e-Islam (S)") party and son of [Sami-ul-Haq](/wiki/Sami-ul-Haq "Sami-ul-Haq"), are killed and twenty others are injured in a [suicide bombing](/wiki/Suicide_bombing "Suicide bombing") inside of a [mosque](/wiki/Mosque "Mosque") in [Khyber Pakhtunkhwa](/wiki/Khyber_Pakhtunkhwa "Khyber Pakhtunkhwa"), [Pakistan](/wiki/Pakistan "Pakistan"). [(*The Indian Express*)](https://indianexpress.com/article/pakistan/injured-blast-islamic-seminary-training-taliban-9861319/)
* [Mexican drug war](/wiki/Mexican_drug_war "Mexican drug war")
  + At least four people are shot dead in a mechanical workshop in [Coatzacoalcos](/wiki/Coatzacoalcos "Coatzacoalcos"), [Veracruz](/wiki/Veracruz "Veracruz"), [Mexico](/wiki/Mexico "Mexico"). This is the second massacre this week in the state, the other in [Perote](/wiki/Perote%2C_Veracruz "Perote, Veracruz"), which left three workers dead and one wounded. [(La Jornada)](https://www.jornada.com.mx/noticia/2025/02/26/estados/matan-a-tres-en-ataque-armado-en-taller-mecanico-de-veracruz)
  + Three policemen and a civilian are killed in two attacks in [Guanajuato](/wiki/Guanajuato "Guanajuato"), Mexico, the first in [Celaya](/wiki/Celaya "Celaya") and the second in [Apaseo el Alto](/wiki/Apaseo_el_Alto "Apaseo el Alto"). [(*Revista Proceso*)](https://www.proceso.com.mx/nacional/estados/2025/2/28/van-tres-policias-asesinados-en-ataques-armados-dirigidos-en-las-ultimas-24-horas-en-guanajuato-346462.html)

**Business and economy**

* [Protests against Donald Trump](/wiki/Protests_against_Donald_Trump "Protests against Donald Trump")
  + [Protests against the second presidency of Donald Trump](/wiki/Protests_against_the_second_presidency_of_Donald_Trump "Protests against the second presidency of Donald Trump")
    - [Economic Blackout](/wiki/Economic_Blackout "Economic Blackout")
      * A 24-hour [consumer spending](/wiki/Consumer_spending "Consumer spending") [boycott](/wiki/Boycott "Boycott") takes place across the [United States](/wiki/United_States "United States"), in protest of wealth and [income inequality](/wiki/Income_distribution "Income distribution"), high prices of essential goods, and the rollback of [diversity, equity, and inclusion](/wiki/Diversity%2C_equity%2C_and_inclusion "Diversity, equity, and inclusion") initiatives by the [Trump administration](/wiki/Second_presidency_of_Donald_Trump "Second presidency of Donald Trump"). [(AP)](https://apnews.com/article/feb-28-economic-blackout-2025-d6b0bf2d1c989ee3071016e36598d76c)
* [2025 United States federal mass layoffs](/wiki/2025_United_States_federal_mass_layoffs "2025 United States federal mass layoffs")
  + The [United States](/wiki/United_States "United States") [Social Security Administration](/wiki/Social_Security_Administration "Social Security Administration") announces it will [lay off](/wiki/Layoff "Layoff") over 7,000 jobs to align with [President](/wiki/U.S._President "U.S. President") [Donald Trump](/wiki/Donald_Trump "Donald Trump")'s [executive order](/wiki/Executive_order "Executive order"), despite its workforce already being at a 50-year low. [(NPR)](https://www.npr.org/2025/02/28/nx-s1-5296986/trump-worker-cuts-social-security-administration)

**Disasters and accidents**

* [2024–25 South-West Indian Ocean cyclone season](/wiki/2024%E2%80%9325_South-West_Indian_Ocean_cyclone_season "2024–25 South-West Indian Ocean cyclone season")
  + Three people are killed as [tropical cyclone](/wiki/Tropical_cyclone "Tropical cyclone") [Garance](/wiki/2024%E2%80%9325_South-West_Indian_Ocean_cyclone_season#Intense_Tropical_Cyclone_Garance "2024–25 South-West Indian Ocean cyclone season") makes landfall in [Réunion](/wiki/R%C3%A9union "Réunion") in the [Indian Ocean](/wiki/Indian_Ocean "Indian Ocean"). [(AP)](https://apnews.com/article/reunion-island-cyclone-garance-damages-d20ddf429639502e67f97089626bc7ec)
* [2025 disease outbreak in the Democratic Republic of the Congo](/wiki/2025_disease_outbreak_in_the_Democratic_Republic_of_the_Congo "2025 disease outbreak in the Democratic Republic of the Congo")
  + At least 60 fatalities and nearly 1,100 symptomatic cases are reported to be a result of a disease outbreak of unknown etiology in the [Province of Équateur](/wiki/Province_of_%C3%89quateur "Province of Équateur"), [Democratic Republic of the Congo](/wiki/Democratic_Republic_of_the_Congo "Democratic Republic of the Congo"). [(CBS News)](https://www.cbsnews.com/news/congo-mystery-disease-deaths-who-investigation-deepens/)

**Health and environment**

* [2025 Southwest United States measles outbreak](/wiki/2025_Southwest_United_States_measles_outbreak "2025 Southwest United States measles outbreak")
  + The number of [measles](/wiki/Measles "Measles") cases in [Texas](/wiki/Texas "Texas"), United States, increases to 146 with 20 people hospitalized, spanning nine [counties](/wiki/List_of_counties_in_Texas "List of counties in Texas") in the state. [(AP)](https://apnews.com/article/measles-outbreak-texas-vaccination-rfk-7e1df8310d6e139010ab7f4e4069c199)

**International relations**

* [Ukraine–United States relations](/wiki/Ukraine%E2%80%93United_States_relations "Ukraine–United States relations")
  + [Peace negotiations in the Russian invasion of Ukraine](/wiki/Peace_negotiations_in_the_Russian_invasion_of_Ukraine "Peace negotiations in the Russian invasion of Ukraine")
    - [2025 Trump–Zelenskyy meeting](/wiki/2025_Trump%E2%80%93Zelenskyy_meeting "2025 Trump–Zelenskyy meeting")
      * [U.S. president](/wiki/U.S._president "U.S. president") [Donald Trump](/wiki/Donald_Trump "Donald Trump"), [U.S. vice president](/wiki/U.S._vice_president "U.S. vice president") [JD Vance](/wiki/JD_Vance "JD Vance") and [Ukrainian president](/wiki/President_of_Ukraine "President of Ukraine") [Volodymyr Zelenskyy](/wiki/Volodymyr_Zelenskyy "Volodymyr Zelenskyy") end their talks early after their meeting in the [White House](/wiki/White_House "White House") turns into a "heated" exchange. Trump rejects any discussion of specific security guarantees for [Ukraine](/wiki/Ukraine "Ukraine"), being interested solely in discussing the [Ukraine–United States Mineral Resources Agreement](/wiki/Ukraine%E2%80%93United_States_Mineral_Resources_Agreement "Ukraine–United States Mineral Resources Agreement"). [(*Time*)](https://time.com/7262883/trump-zelensky-meeting/) [(AP)](https://apnews.com/article/zelenskyy-security-guarantees-trump-meeting-washington-eebdf97b663c2cdc9e51fa346b09591d)
      * The [U.S. State Department](/wiki/United_States_Department_of_State "United States Department of State") terminates U.S. support of [Ukraine's energy grid](/wiki/Energy_in_Ukraine "Energy in Ukraine") restoration amid an ongoing [energy crisis](/wiki/Ukrainian_energy_crisis "Ukrainian energy crisis"). [(NBC)](https://www.nbcnews.com/politics/state-department-terminates-us-support-ukraine-energy-grid-restoration-rcna194259)
* [Colombia–Israel relations](/wiki/Colombia%E2%80%93Israel_relations "Colombia–Israel relations"), [Israel–Malaysia relations](/wiki/Israel%E2%80%93Malaysia_relations "Israel–Malaysia relations"), [South Africa–Israel relations](/wiki/South_Africa%E2%80%93Israel_relations "South Africa–Israel relations"), [Boycotts of Israel](/wiki/Boycotts_of_Israel "Boycotts of Israel")
  + [Colombian](/wiki/Colombia "Colombia") [president](/wiki/President_of_Colombia "President of Colombia") [Gustavo Petro](/wiki/Gustavo_Petro "Gustavo Petro"), [Malaysian](/wiki/Malaysia "Malaysia") [prime minister](/wiki/Prime_Minister_of_Malaysia "Prime Minister of Malaysia") [Anwar Ibrahim](/wiki/Anwar_Ibrahim "Anwar Ibrahim"), and [South African](/wiki/South_Africa "South Africa") [president](/wiki/President_of_South_Africa "President of South Africa") [Cyril Ramaphosa](/wiki/Cyril_Ramaphosa "Cyril Ramaphosa") release a joint statement announcing they will close their [ports](/wiki/Port "Port") to any ship carrying [weapons supplied to Israel](/wiki/Israel%27s_arms_supplier_countries "Israel's arms supplier countries"). [(Middle East Monitor)](https://www.middleeastmonitor.com/20250228-south-africa-malaysia-colombia-condemn-trumps-gaza-riviera-plan-as-ethnic-cleansing/)
* [Democratic Republic of the Congo–Rwanda conflict](/wiki/Democratic_Republic_of_the_Congo%E2%80%93Rwanda_conflict_%282022%E2%80%93present%29 "Democratic Republic of the Congo–Rwanda conflict (2022–present)")
  + The [East African Community](/wiki/East_African_Community "East African Community") (EAC) and the [Southern African Development Community](/wiki/Southern_African_Development_Community "Southern African Development Community") (SADC) postpone the joint summit of their foreign ministers that would have agreed on a ceasefire plan for the conflict in the eastern [Democratic Republic of the Congo](/wiki/Democratic_Republic_of_the_Congo "Democratic Republic of the Congo"). The Congolese and [Rwanda](/wiki/Rwanda "Rwanda") governments never received invitations to the meeting. [(Critical Threats Project)](https://www.criticalthreats.org/briefs/congo-war-security-review/congo-war-security-review-february-28-2025)
* [Russia–United States relations](/wiki/Russia%E2%80%93United_States_relations "Russia–United States relations")
  + [Russia](/wiki/Russia "Russia") appoints [Alexander Darchiev](/wiki/Alexander_Darchiev "Alexander Darchiev") as its new [ambassador to the U.S.](/wiki/List_of_ambassadors_of_Russia_to_the_United_States "List of ambassadors of Russia to the United States") following talks between the two countries in [Istanbul](/wiki/Istanbul "Istanbul") on restoring regular diplomatic contacts and embassy staffs. The post has been vacant for several months. [(Barron's)](https://www.barrons.com/news/russia-names-new-ambassador-to-us-after-istanbul-talks-e9993f36) [(Interfax)](https://interfax.com/newsroom/top-stories/110109/)

**Law and crime**

* Mexico extradites 29 alleged cartel members to the United States, including [Rafael Caro Quintero](/wiki/Rafael_Caro_Quintero "Rafael Caro Quintero"), [Miguel Treviño Morales](/wiki/Miguel_Trevi%C3%B1o_Morales "Miguel Treviño Morales"), [Omar Treviño Morales](/wiki/Omar_Trevi%C3%B1o_Morales "Omar Treviño Morales"), [Vicente Carrillo Fuentes](/wiki/Vicente_Carrillo_Fuentes "Vicente Carrillo Fuentes") and [Jose Rodolfo Villarreal-Hernandez](/wiki/Jose_Rodolfo_Villarreal-Hernandez "Jose Rodolfo Villarreal-Hernandez"). [(BBC News)](https://www.bbc.com/news/articles/cx2995y25lyo) [(CBS News)](https://www.cbsnews.com/texas/news/cartel-boss-el-gato-extradited-us-2013-north-texas-murder/)

**Politics and elections**

* [Greeks](/wiki/Greeks "Greeks") organize a 24-hour nationwide [general strike](/wiki/General_strike "General strike") on the second anniversary of the [Tempi train crash](/wiki/Tempi_train_crash "Tempi train crash"), [Greece](/wiki/Greece "Greece")'s deadliest railway disaster. [(Reuters)](https://www.reuters.com/world/europe/greece-standstill-ahead-mass-protest-anniversary-deadly-train-crash-2025-02-28/)
* Following the [2024 quota reform movement](/wiki/2024_Bangladesh_quota_reform_movement "2024 Bangladesh quota reform movement") in [Bangladesh](/wiki/Bangladesh "Bangladesh"), students who led the protests announce the formation of a new political party, the [National Citizen Party](/wiki/National_Citizen_Party_%28Bangladesh%29 "National Citizen Party (Bangladesh)"), led by [Nahid Islam](/wiki/Nahid_Islam "Nahid Islam"), a [student activist](/wiki/Student_activist "Student activist") and the chief coordinator of the [Students Against Discrimination](/wiki/Students_Against_Discrimination "Students Against Discrimination") movement. [(DW)](https://www.dw.com/en/bangladesh-students-launch-new-party-to-shake-up-politics/a-71786361)

**Science and technology**

* [Microsoft](/wiki/Microsoft "Microsoft") announces it will shut down [Skype](/wiki/Skype "Skype") in May 2025 to focus its support and development on [Teams](/wiki/Microsoft_Teams "Microsoft Teams"). [(DW)](https://www.dw.com/en/microsoft-to-retire-skype-in-favor-of-teams/a-71786197) [(Bloomberg News)](https://www.bloomberg.com/news/articles/2025-02-28/microsoft-msft-to-shut-down-skype-as-zoom-teams-dominate-video-calls)
